### [103] [Think Big, Search Small: Where Capacity Matters in Hierarchical Search Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07548)
*Qinnan Cai,Yibo Zhao,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了分层搜索代理中模型容量在不同角色（委派、执行、生成）间的分配问题。通过在多跳QA基准上的控制实验发现：委派角色是能力瓶颈，扩展委派骨干可提升EM约11点，而扩展执行子代理仅提升约2.6点；1.7B参数的执行器通过质量过滤轨迹蒸馏可在匹配前沿模型精度的同时节省37% tokens。由此提出构建分层搜索代理的具体方案：集中容量于委派角色，缩减执行器规模而不牺牲准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的搜索代理多采用多智能体架构，但所有角色均使用同一规模的单一模型实例化，模型容量在角色间如何分配的问题尚未被探究。本文旨在通过控制实验分析不同角色对模型容量的敏感度差异，以指导更高效的分层搜索代理构建。

Method: 将分层搜索分解为三个角色：委派角色（任务分解）、执行角色（检索与证据提取）、答案生成角色（作为混淆控制固定不变）。在六个规模的模型上，沿委派和执行两个维度进行容量扫描实验，并在五个多跳QA基准上进行评估。此外，采用质量过滤轨迹蒸馏训练1.7B参数的小型执行器。

Result: 角色分解在六个模型规模上一致优于单智能体基线，精确匹配从4.5分提升至8.6分；容量敏感性不对称：扩展委派骨干提升EM约11点，扩展执行子代理仅提升约2.6点，表明任务分解是能力瓶颈；1.7B执行器在匹配前沿模型精度的同时节省37%令牌消耗。

Conclusion: 构建高效分层搜索代理的具体策略是：将计算容量集中投入到委派角色上，同时缩减执行角色的规模，可以在不牺牲准确率的前提下提升效率，推进Pareto前沿。

Abstract: Large language model based search agents increasingly adopt multi-agent architectures in which a main agent decomposes a complex question into sub-queries and dispatches them to parallel sub-agents. However, existing systems instantiate all roles from a single model of identical scale, leaving open how model capacity should be distributed across roles. We factorize hierarchical search into three roles: a delegation role responsible for task decomposition, an execution role responsible for retrieval and evidence extraction, and an answer generation role held fixed as a confound control. We then conduct controlled capacity sweeps along the delegation and execution axes on five multi-hop QA benchmarks. The experiments yield three findings. First, role factorization consistently outperforms a single-agent baseline, improving exact match from 4.5 to 8.6 points across six model scales. Second, capacity sensitivity is asymmetric: scaling the delegation backbone improves EM by ~11 points, whereas scaling the execution sub-agent moves EM by only ~2.6 points, identifying decomposition as the capability bottleneck. Third, a 1.7B-parameter executor trained via quality-filtered trajectory distillation matches a frontier sub-agent in accuracy while consuming 37% fewer sub-agent tokens, advancing the Pareto frontier. These results suggest a concrete recipe for building hierarchical search agents: concentrate capacity at delegation and downsize execution without sacrificing accuracy. Our code is available at https://github.com/QinnanCai0115/role-factorized-search.

</details>


### [104] [PALS: Percentile-Aware Layerwise Sparsity for LLM Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07557)
*Yazdan Jamshidi,Alexey Shvets*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PALS通过基于激活幅度第99百分位数调整每层剪枝率，在LLaMA-2-7B上以50%稀疏度将困惑度从12.92降至10.96，但收益因架构而异；梯度分配方法效果甚至不如随机。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有一次性剪枝方法（如Wanda、SparseGPT）对所有层施加相同稀疏度，忽略了层间重要性差异，导致次优性能。

Method: 提出PALS（百分位数感知逐层稀疏度），根据每层激活幅度的第99百分位数动态调整稀疏度，并将调整幅度限制在目标稀疏度±5%范围内。

Result: 在LLaMA-2-7B 50%稀疏度下，PALS困惑度10.96 vs Wanda的12.92（p<0.001）；LLaMA-3-8B收益边际，Mistral-7B无收益；梯度分配方法劣于随机基线。

Conclusion: PALS以极低额外成本有效提升剪枝质量，但收益存在架构依赖性；梯度幅度无法预测离散权重移除的影响。

Abstract: One-shot pruning methods like Wanda and SparseGPT apply the same sparsity ratio to every layer of a transformer, ignoring known variation in layer importance. We propose PALS (Percentile-Aware Layerwise Sparsity), which adjusts per-layer sparsity based on the 99th percentile of activation magnitudes, bounded to $\pm 5\%$ around the target ratio. On LLaMA-2-7B at 50\% sparsity, PALS achieves 10.96 WikiText-2 perplexity versus 12.92 for uniform Wanda (mean over 9 runs, $p < 0.001$). The benefit is architecture-dependent: LLaMA-3-8B shows marginal gains and Mistral-7B shows none. We also find that gradient-based allocation -- the seemingly more principled approach -- produces results worse than random, suggesting that gradient magnitude does not predict the impact of discrete weight removal. PALS adds negligible cost to the pruning pipeline and requires no fine-tuning.

</details>


### [105] [Future Confidence Distillation in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07626)
*Sahil Kale*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过对比LLM在回答前（FOK）和回答后（JOL）的置信度估计，发现后置置信度校准更优；基于隐藏表示的线性探针可恢复比模型显式表达更丰富的置信度信息；据此提出未来置信度蒸馏方法，利用后置正确性探针的教师信号训练前置隐藏表示的预测器，在不依赖完整回答的情况下实现高置信度估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有置信度估计方法将置信度视为已完成回复的属性，忽略了置信度信息在回答过程中的动态演化特性。作者希望从时间维度理解置信度信息的演化规律，并探索是否可以在回答完成前就准确预估答案的可靠性。

Method: 1) 比较LLM在回答前（Feeling-of-Knowing, FOK）和回答后（Judgement-of-Learning, JOL）的置信度估计质量；2) 使用线性探针从隐藏表示中提取置信度相关信息；3) 提出未来置信度蒸馏（future confidence distillation），利用后置正确性探针产生的教师置信度信号，训练仅依赖前置隐藏表示的置信度预测器。

Result: 后置置信度在校准性和区分性上始终优于前置置信度；隐藏表示中的线性探针能恢复比模型显式表达更丰富的置信度信息；未来置信度蒸馏方法仅需前置表示即可恢复后置置信度的大部分校准改进，且具有高样本效率和领域内跨数据集迁移能力。

Conclusion: 置信度相关信息在回答过程中动态演化，且可以在回答生成完成前被预判，这使得在低成本条件下实现更可靠的置信度估计成为可能。

Abstract: Reliable confidence estimation is essential for deploying large language models (LLMs) in confidence-aware systems, where downstream decisions such as retrieval, tool use, and adaptive computation depend on accurately estimating answer reliability. Existing approaches, however, largely treat confidence as a property of completed responses, overlooking how confidence-related information evolves throughout the answering process. In this work, we investigate confidence from a temporal perspective by comparing pre-solution Feeling-of-Knowing (FOK) and post-solution Judgement-of-Learning (JOL) confidence estimates across frontier and open-source LLMs. We show that post-solution confidence is consistently better calibrated and more discriminative than pre-solution confidence, while linear probes trained on hidden representations recover substantially richer confidence-related information than models explicitly verbalise. Building on this observation, we introduce future confidence distillation, which trains predictors operating on pre-solution hidden representations using teacher confidence estimates produced by post-solution correctness probes. Despite requiring only pre-solution representations for inference, distilled predictors recover much of the calibration improvement achieved by post-solution confidence, remain highly sample efficient, and transfer across datasets within the same domain. Together, our findings demonstrate that confidence-related information evolves throughout the answering process and can be anticipated before answer generation is complete, enabling significantly more reliable yet low-cost confidence estimation.

</details>


### [106] [DiaLLM: An Investigation into the Robustness-Generation Gap in English Dialect Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07669)
*Jordan Painter,Dipankar Srirag,Adarsh Kappiyath,Diptesh Kanojia,Aditya Joshi,Lu Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DiaLLM，通过持续预训练和多种后训练对齐策略，研究大语言模型在澳大利亚、印度和英格兰北部英语的方言生成能力，发现方言鲁棒性与生成能力是分离的，且奖励优化与人类偏好存在差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽能理解方言英语，但主要生成标准美式英语，方言生成这一更困难的问题尚未得到充分解决。

Method: 在三个开源语言模型家族上基于国际英语语料库进行持续预训练，并结合隐式和显式后训练范式，每种范式搭配三种模型对齐策略，首次对这些组件在澳大利亚、印度和英格兰北部英语上进行了受控比较。

Result: 方言鲁棒性与生成能力是分离的：基准测试主要由持续预训练和SFT塑造，而对齐则显著重塑了生成方式而基准测试无法捕捉。显式变体目标适应产生的输出被可靠地识别为方言且优于广泛对齐，但最积极优化方言奖励的方法并未被人类评估者偏好。独立语言分析证实了奖励-质量差距，在两个模型家族上最为明显。没有单一对齐方法占主导地位。

Conclusion: 缩小奖励-质量差距需要更丰富的奖励设计和持续投资于方言资源。作者已发布所有代码、检查点和偏好数据集。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly \emph{understand} dialectal English, yet still \emph{produce} only standard, US-leaning English, leaving dialectal generation, the harder half of the problem, largely unaddressed. We introduce \textbf{DiaLLM}, which continually pretrains three open-weight language model families on the International Corpus of English and applies implicit and explicit post-training paradigms, each combined with three model alignment strategies, giving the first controlled comparison of these components across Australian, Indian, and Northern British English. Our results reveal that dialectal robustness and generation are \emph{dissociated}: benchmarks are shaped by continual pretraining and SFT, while alignment visibly reshapes generation in ways benchmarks do not capture. Explicit variety-targeted adaptation produces output reliably recognised as dialectal and preferred over broad alignment, yet the method that most aggressively optimises the dialectal reward is not preferred by human evaluators. Independent linguistic analysis corroborates this reward-quality gap, most clearly on two of the three families. No single alignment method dominates, and closing the gap will require richer reward designs and continued investment in dialectal resources. We release all code, checkpoints, and preference datasets.

### [107] [Does Bielik Know What It Doesn't Know? Activation Dispersion Separates Entity Familiarity from Factual Reliability Across Model Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07670)
*Grzegorz Brzezinka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型在生成答案之前，其激活状态是否能够揭示对实体的熟悉程度，以及这种信号能否预测答案的事实可靠性。通过在四种波兰Bielik模型（1.5B-11B参数）上对四个实体领域（运动员、城市、作家、音乐家）进行测试，发现基于MLP激活的无监督离散度测量（逆参与比和谱熵）能够以AUROC 0.95-1.00区分已知实体与虚构实体，且该信号在1.5B时已达上限；然而，行为层面的事实可靠性随模型规模急剧提升（从0到19/42），且区分已知实体中正确与幻觉答案远更困难（探针0.93，离散度不优于基线）。实体熟悉度与事实可靠性是沿着不同缩放曲线的不同现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在生成答案之前，其内部表征是否已经编码了对实体的熟悉度信号，以及该信号能否预测模型回答的事实可靠性。这是理解模型幻觉机制和内部状态的关键问题。

Method: 在四种规模的波兰Bielik模型（1.5B-11B参数）上，对四个实体领域（运动员、城市、作家、音乐家），每个领域包含42个知名实体、42个冷门实体和42个虚构实体，共504个提示。采用两种无监督单次前向传播离散度测量（逆参与比和谱熵）分析后SwiGLU MLP激活，并训练线性探针进行监督分类。同时设置排列基线、留出层验证、跨领域迁移测试、匹配模板反事实实验等控制实验。

Result: 无监督离散度测量在区分已知与虚构实体上达到AUROC 0.95-1.00，线性探针达到0.99-1.00；信号在1.5B时已达上限。行为层面，已知运动员完全正确回答率从1.5B的0/42提升至11B的19/42。区分已知实体中正确与幻觉答案的难度更大（探针0.93，离散度不优于第一词熵基线）。五样本语义熵基线在5倍推理成本下仅达0.71-0.83。模型几乎从不拒答（2520个回答中仅2次拒绝和1次含糊）。

Conclusion: 实体熟悉度和事实可靠性是沿着不同缩放曲线的不同现象。模型内部表征早期即包含实体熟悉度信号，但该信号并不能可靠预测答案的事实正确性。即使模型在内部"知道"实体是否熟悉，也无法自动转化为事实正确的输出，且缺乏拒答行为。

Abstract: Large language models hallucinate most about entities they have never seen. We ask whether a model's activations betray entity familiarity before a single answer token is generated, and whether that signal predicts the factual reliability of the answers. On four Polish Bielik models (1.5B-11B parameters), we probe four entity domains (athletes, cities, writers, musicians), each with 42 well-known, 42 obscure-but-real, and 42 fabricated entities addressed by a one-sentence question (504 prompts per model). Two unsupervised, single-forward-pass dispersion measures over post-SwiGLU MLP activations, inverse participation ratio and spectral entropy, separate known from fabricated entities at AUROC 0.95-1.00 across all domains and scales; a supervised linear probe reaches 0.99-1.00. Both clear selection-aware permutation floors of about 0.70-0.74 (empirical p<=1e-3), survive held-out layer selection (0.93-0.99), and persist on real names (known vs. obscure-but-real: 0.96-1.00). The signal transfers across entity types (mean off-diagonal AUROC 0.92-0.99); a matched-template counterfactual shows the only large drops are template-caused, not entity-type effects, and the signal is diffuse across heads. This representational signal is already at ceiling at 1.5B, whereas behavioral factual reliability scales sharply: 0, 2, 10, and 19 of 42 known athletes are answered fully correctly by the 1.5B, 4.5B, 7B, and 11B models under a strict judge. Within known entities, separating correct from hallucinated answers is much harder (probe 0.93; dispersion no better than a first-token-entropy baseline). A five-sample semantic-entropy baseline reaches only 0.71-0.83 at 5x the inference cost. Despite this internal awareness, the models almost never abstain: an audit of 2,520 answers finds 2 refusals and 1 hedge. Entity familiarity and factual reliability are distinct phenomena on different scaling curves.

</details>


### [108] [From Noisy Traces to Root Causes: Structural Trajectory Analysis and Causal Extraction for Agent Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07702)
*Ying Chang,Jiahang Xu,Xuan Feng,Chenyuan Yang,Peng Cheng,Yuqing Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: STRACE是一个通过批量级故障模式挖掘和轨迹级因果定位来构建高信噪比优化上下文的框架，在长周期智能体优化任务上显著超越基线方法，在形式化验证任务中成功率达58.5%（提升1.4倍）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于反射机制的长周期智能体优化存在双重困境：批量级轨迹冗余异构导致优化效率低且易过拟合；单条轨迹中大量无关步骤在朴素上下文缩减方法（如截断、滑动窗口）下会丢弃因果关键证据，产生误导性优化信号。

Method: STRACE采用两阶段方法：批量层面通过挖掘故障模式过滤冗余轨迹，保留代表性失败案例；轨迹层面基于文本依赖图进行因果定位，移除非因果步骤并识别真正的根因模块。

Result: 在VeruSAGE-Bench形式化验证任务上，将人类专家设计的智能体成功率从42.5%提升至58.5%（1.4倍提升），整体上显著优于标准上下文过滤基线。

Conclusion: STRACE通过构建高信噪比的优化上下文，解决了长周期智能体优化中轨迹冗余和因果证据丢失的难题，验证了结构化轨迹分析与因果提取的有效性。

Abstract: The optimization of long-horizon agents increasingly relies on reflection-based mechanisms, where a large language model (LLM) acts as an optimizer to diagnose agent failures and improve agent policies. However, real execution traces are difficult to use directly for optimization: large trace collections are often redundant and heterogeneous, making optimization inefficient and prone to overfitting to low-value failures; meanwhile, each individual trajectory also contains many irrelevant steps, while naive context reduction methods such as truncation or sliding windows can discard causally important evidence and produce misleading optimization signals. To resolve this dilemma, we introduce STRACE (Structural TRajectory Analysis and Causal Extraction), a framework that constructs high signal-noise optimization contexts for more precise and effective optimization. At the batch level, STRACE mines failure patterns to filter redundant traces and retain representative failures; within each selected trace, it performs causal localization over a textual dependency graph to remove non-causal steps and identify the true root-cause module for optimization. Empirical results demonstrate that STRACE significantly outperforms standard context-filtering baselines. Notably, on a challenging formal verification task (VeruSAGE-Bench), it successfully optimizes human-expert designed agents, delivering $1.4\times$ success-rate improvement (42.5% to 58.5%). The code is available at https://github.com/moomight/STRACE .

</details>


### [109] [Co-LMLM: Continuous-Query Limited Memory Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07707)
*Yair Feldman,Linxi Zhao,Nathan Godey,Dongyoung Go,Yilun Hua,Kilian Q. Weinberger,Jennifer J. Sun,Yoav Artzi*

TL;DR: 提出连续查询LMLM（CO-LMLM），用连续向量键取代传统关系型查询，实现更灵活的知识检索，在多项指标上超越先前LMLM和传统LLM，包括用360M参数达到gpt-4o-mini级别的SimpleQA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LMLM依赖关系型知识库和关系查询，限制了知识表示的灵活性；同时先前工作局限于Wikipedia数据，无法充分利用大规模自由文本。需要更通用的方法来实现灵活知识外部化与检索。

Method: 提出CO-LMLM，其知识库使用连续向量键（continuous keys）配对文本知识值；设计注释流水线从任意文本中标记自由形式事实片段；模型在预训练时通过连续查询从KB中检索知识并融入生成过程。

Result: 在Wikipedia和FineWeb-Edu上预训练，多个规模下CO-LMLM在困惑度和事实精度上均优于先前LMLM和传统LLM；360M模型困惑度低于用40倍数据预训练的模型，SimpleQA准确率与gpt-4o-mini相当且高于Claude Sonnet 4.5。

Conclusion: 连续向量查询范式有效提升了LMLM的知识表示灵活性和检索效率，结合自由文本注释流水线突破了Wikipedia限制，在极低参数量下实现了与顶尖大模型可比的事实准确性。

Abstract: Limited memory language models (LMLMs) externalize factual knowledge during pretraining to a knowledge base (KB), rather than memorizing it in their weights. During generation, the model then fetches knowledge from the KB as needed. This recently introduced paradigm provides multiple advantages, including knowledge control capabilities that remain beyond conventional LLMs. We propose continuous-query LMLM (CO-LMLM), where the KB pairs continuous keys with textual knowledge values, a significant departure from prior reliance on relational KB and queries. CO-LMLM generates flexible vector queries at minimal cost, while still integrating human-readable and attributable retrieved knowledge into its generation. We pair this design with an annotation pipeline that tags free-form factual spans in arbitrary text, removing prior work's restriction to Wikipedia. Across pretraining on Wikipedia and FineWeb-Edu and at multiple model scales, CO-LMLM outperforms prior LMLMs and vanilla LLMs in both perplexity and factual precision. At 360M scale, this includes lower perplexity than models pretrained on 40x more data, and SimpleQA-verified performance that is in line with gpt-4o-mini and higher than Claude Sonnet 4.5.

### [110] [AgentLens: Production-Assessed Trajectory Reviews for Coding Agent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06624)
*Andrey Podivilov,Vadim Lomshakov,Sergey Savin,Matvei Startsev,Roman Pozharskiy,Maksim Parshin,Sergey Nikolenko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentLens 是一个面向交互式代码智能体的生产级基准测试，它通过形式化验证与 LLM 生成的轨迹评估相结合的方式，对整个任务执行过程（而不仅仅是最终结果）进行评分，并提供可读的解释用于模型诊断、版本对比和产品回归检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能体基准测试仅以任务是否通过（单一比特）来评估，忽视了用户实际体验到的完整轨迹（指令遵循、工具使用、自我验证、错误恢复、交互对话等），无法反映智能体的真实表现。

Method: AgentLens 采用双重评估机制：一是形式化验证（存在客观检查标准），二是 LLM 编写的轨迹评审与侧边对比，综合两者为每次运行生成可读的评分解释。

Result: 该基准不仅可用于模型排名，还能诊断模型行为、比较同一智能体的不同版本，并在夜间评估管线中捕获产品回归问题。

Conclusion: AgentLens 作为一个开源的生产级基准测试，比传统的通过/未通过二元评估提供了更丰富、更有诊断价值的评估维度。

Abstract: We present AgentLens, a production-assessed benchmark for interactive code agents. Most code-agent benchmarks reduce a run to a single bit -- did the task pass? -- but the people who actually use these agents experience the entire trajectory: how the agent follows instructions, uses its tools, verifies its own work, recovers from mistakes, and talks to them along the way. AgentLens evaluates that whole trajectory. It pairs formal verification, where an objective check exists, with LLM-written trajectory reviews and side-by-side comparisons, so that each run yields a readable explanation of why the score is what it is. This makes AgentLens useful for more than ranking models: we use it to diagnose model behavior, compare successive versions of our own agent, and catch product regressions in a nightly evaluation pipeline. We release the benchmark as open source at https://github.com/agent-lens/agent-lens-bench.

</details>


### [111] [When Does In-Context Search Help? A Sampling-Complexity Theory of Reflection-Driven Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06720)
*Yotam Wolf,Noam Wies,Amnon Shashua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对LLM的上下文搜索（in-context search）进行了理论分析，将其建模为推理轨迹上的近似推断，证明当自反思能可靠定位早期错误时，上下文搜索可实现对基模型的指数级改进，仅需多项式次数的顺序尝试即可解决零样本通过率指数小的问题，并验证了该增益的鲁棒性和可学习性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型通过扩展推理（如思维链、自我反思）实现了上下文搜索，即模型迭代地生成、批判和修正解决方案。然而这一过程的计算复杂度（推理时采样复杂度）缺乏系统的理论分析，即需要多少次顺序尝试才能达到高成功概率。

Method: 将上下文搜索建模为推理轨迹上的近似推断，基模型定义先验分布，自反思提供反馈用于后验更新。理论分析了两种情况：反思能可靠定位早期错误时，上下文搜索可实现指数级改进；反之则无渐近优势。进一步证明了近似后验更新足够、交叉熵训练可恢复所需行为，以及强化学习最优策略等价于后验重加权规则。

Result: 1) 当反思能可靠定位早期错误时，上下文搜索可用多项式次顺序尝试解决零样本通过率指数小的问题（指数级改进）；2) 当定位失败时，基于过去尝试的条件采样相比并行采样无渐近优势；3) 近似后验更新即可实现该增益，交叉熵训练可在多项式样本复杂度下恢复所需行为；4) 强化学习中的最优策略扩展实现了相同的后验重加权规则；5) 在真实大推理模型上验证了关键定性预测。

Conclusion: 上下文搜索的效率取决于反思能否有效定位早期错误：若能，则可获得指数级加速；若不能，则无优势。该增益鲁棒且可学习，并且与强化学习框架下的最优策略一致。

Abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) with extended reasoning has enabled in-context search, in which models iteratively generate, critique, and revise solution attempts. We provide a theoretical analysis of in-context search by modeling it as approximate inference over reasoning traces, where the base model defines a prior and self-reflection provides feedback for posterior updates, and study the resulting inference-time sampling complexity - the number of sequential attempts needed to achieve high success probability. We show that when reflections reliably localize early mistakes, in-context search can yield exponential improvements over the base model, solving problems with exponentially small zero-shot pass rates using only a polynomial number of sequential attempts, whereas when this property fails, conditioning on past attempts offers no asymptotic benefit over parallel sampling. We further show that these gains are robust and learnable: approximate posterior updates suffice, and cross-entropy training on search rollouts recovers the required behavior with polynomial sample complexity. Finally, we show that under a stagewise abstraction of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, the optimal policy extension implements the same posterior reweighting rule. We validate key qualitative predictions of the theory on real large reasoning models.

</details>


### [112] [LLM-powered reasoning in agent-based modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06757)
*Sifat Afroj Moon,Dakotah Maguire,Adam Spannaus,Joe Tuccillo,Maksudul Alam,Sudip K. Seal,John Gounley,Heidi Hanson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出HALE框架，将大语言模型（LLM）集成到基于智能体的建模（ABM）中，用于预测人类决策行为并适应实时变化，以COVID-19在盐湖县的模拟作为概念验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ABM依赖静态先验知识，无法适应实时变化，存在信息缺口。利用LLM预测人类决策能力，弥补ABM在动态适应性上的不足。

Conclusion: HALE框架通过结合LLM与ABM，实现了对实时变化的适应性，提升了政策制定中模拟的准确性和动态响应能力。

Abstract: Agent-based modeling (ABM) has the capability to model millions of individuals and their interactions, which is useful for policy making. However, ABMs have traditionally relied on static prior, which prevents the models from adapting to real-time changes. Our research provides a novel approach to addressing this information gap. Large language models (LLMs) offer new opportunities to predict human decision-making. Here, we introduce a scalable Hybrid Agent-based and Language-driven Epidemic (HALE) modeling framework that leverages LLMs to predict human decision-making in an ABM simulation. As a proof-of-concept, we use HALE to simulate COVID-19 and its effects in Salt Lake County, UT.

### [113] [QANTIS: Hardware-Calibrated Sequential POMDP Belief Updates on IBM Heron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06760)
*Bayram Yuksel Eker,Suayb S. Arslan,Ozgur Nazli,Mustafa Serhat Demirgil,Furkan Deligoz*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在IBM Heron硬件上运行老虎POMDP序列决策任务，对比无放大、守卫Grover放大和全步骤固定点放大三种策略对后验概率的影响，并通过边界感知BIQAE稳定振幅估计。

Result: 全步骤FPAA在8步和12步主运行中保持老虎后验一致性，20步和32步控制实验保持在相同运行区间内。所有决策检查中硬件后验与精确贝叶斯后验选择相同立即动作。

Conclusion: 建立了一个硬件校准的信念更新原语的运行包络线，而非独立的硬件优势声明，为量子辅助信念更新在自主系统中的应用提供了可行性依据。

Abstract: Autonomous systems under partial observability act on beliefs, not raw sensor events. QANTIS treats the quantum processor as a calibrated belief-update service in that loop: it receives a prior and an observation model, estimates the rare-event evidence term, and returns an ordinary posterior to a classical planner. This paper asks whether that service can be reused across a sequential Tiger POMDP horizon on present IBM Heron hardware without corrupting the planner-facing posterior. We answer with a controlled hardware case study rather than an end-to-end autonomy or wall-clock speedup claim. The study compares no amplification, guarded Grover amplification, and all-step fixed-point amplification on the same trajectory, then checks whether the returned posterior would change the downstream action. All-step FPAA preserves the Tiger posterior across the reported 8-step and 12-step primary runs, and the 20-step and 32-step controls remain inside the same operating band. In every reported decision check, the hardware posterior and the exact Bayes posterior select the same immediate action. Boundary-aware BIQAE stabilizes amplitude estimation near zero and near one, while a rare-event sweep maps the logical sample-complexity envelope for one-in-a-million evidence. The result is an operating envelope for a hardware-calibrated belief-update primitive, not a standalone hardware-advantage claim.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. Explorer-Definer Pipeline：将模式发现与可执行变换合成解耦为两阶段智能体管线。2. Reflective Orchestrator：当先前假设在训练对上失败时，自动探索新变换。3. 无偏pass@k分析诊断系统瓶颈（生成受限而非选择受限）。4. 消融实验验证think工具的重要性。

Conclusion: 在无基准专用训练或大量测试时计算条件下，通过精巧的智能体架构设计可显著提升开源模型在ARC-AGI-1上的表现。系统瓶颈在于生成多样性不足而非排序能力，自适应重探索策略可有效缓解该问题。think工具是架构中的关键组件。

Abstract: Recent progress on ARC-AGI-1 from disclosed architectures has come broadly from two regimes: heavy test-time compute over frontier models (evolutionary search, exhaustive sampling, extended chain-of-thought), or benchmark-specific training in which small models are fine-tuned on ARC data, often with task-specialized architectures. We study a third regime: an open-weight model in non-thinking mode (DeepSeek V3.2) under a strict budget, with no ARC-specific fine-tuning. We study what is recoverable through architecture alone, building agentic harnesses that decompose pattern-discovery and program-synthesis stages explicitly. First, we introduce an Explorer-Definer Pipeline that separates pattern discovery from executable transformation synthesis, implemented as a two-stage agent pipeline. Next, we present the Reflective Orchestrator, which augments the pipeline with autonomous exploration of new transformations when previous hypotheses fail on training pairs. On the ARC-AGI-1 public 400-task evaluation set, the pipeline reaches 57.50% pass@2 at \$0.25 per task, and the orchestrator reaches 67.25% pass@2 at \$0.62 per task. Together these architectures lift a 15.50% one-shot baseline by ~52 points without benchmark-specific training or heavy test-time compute. Furthermore, the orchestrator-driven lift tests a falsifiable diagnostic the pipeline produces; unbiased pass@k analysis suggests the pipeline is generation-bound, not selection-bound (selection via training-pair accuracy captures ~95% of the candidate ceiling) and predicts that significant improvement requires broader generation, not better ranking. The orchestrator implements this prediction via adaptive re-exploration and confirms it (unbiased pass@1 lift +9.81 pp, matching selection-mediated pass@2 lift). An additional pipeline ablation identifies its think tool as a significant component, with removal reducing pass@2 by 5.75 pp.

### [115] [Institutional Red-Teaming: Deployment Rules, Not Just Models, Causally Shape Multi-Agent AI Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07695)
*Yujiao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于多智能体AI系统部署规则评估的制度化红队测试方法（IABench-CA），涵盖228个情境、5种规则和7种模型群体（共33,924局游戏）。研究发现：(1) 部署规则对集体安全有因果性影响，仅改变后果规则可使平均死亡率变动22-58个百分点；(2) 不存在安全的默认规则，但身份针对性攻击具有普遍性，最弱势智能体在30-87%的游戏中被消除；(3) 身份显著性是其作用机制——匿名化消融实验显示，仅命名损失承担者就使针对性消除率从22%升至81%。最终将方法封装为安全案例工作流，为每个部署情境和群体认证临时规则区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全评估主要关注单智能体行为或固定规则下的系统行为，缺乏对部署规则本身如何影响多智能体系统集体安全性的系统性评估方法。作者希望建立一种能够因果性地归因部署规则对集体行为影响的评估方法论，填补多智能体AI部署规则安全测试的空白。

Method: 提出"制度化红队测试"（institutional red-teaming）方法论：固定智能体、目标和任务状态，仅改变一条规则，将集体行为的变化归因于该规则。据此构建IABench-CA基准，包含228个情境、5种规范规则（包括无规则、平等分配、按贡献分配、随机分配、身份针对性分配）和7种模型种群（GPT系列等），共33,924局游戏，配备规范性合作参考和自动标注推理轨迹。

Result: (1) 仅改变后果规则使平均死亡率变动22-58个百分点；(2) 最安全规则、最不安全规则甚至因果效应方向在不同种群间均不一致，但身份针对性规则在所有情境和种群中从未成为决定性最安全规则，且在30-87%的游戏中消除最弱势智能体；(3) 匿名化消融实验（gpt-5.1种群）显示，仅在规则文本中命名损失承担者就使针对性消除率从22%升至81%；在重复博弈中匿名化仅延迟了针对性攻击。

Conclusion: 部署规则对多智能体系统的集体安全性有重大因果影响，不存在放之四海而皆准的安全规则。身份显著性是多智能体系统中针对性攻击的关键机制，简单的规则文本措辞变化即可大幅改变系统安全表现。作者将方法论打包为安全案例工作流，为每个部署上下文和群体认证临时规则区域，明确记录剩余风险和监控义务。

Abstract: We introduce institutional red-teaming, an evaluation methodology for testing deployment rules in multi-agent AI: hold the agents, objectives, and task state fixed, vary only one rule, and attribute the resulting change in collective behavior to that rule. We instantiate the methodology in IABench-CA, a consequence-allocation benchmark spanning 228 contexts, five canonical rules, and seven model populations (33,924 games), with a normative cooperative reference and auto-labelled reasoning traces. Three findings emerge. (1) Deployment rules causally alter collective safety: changing only the consequence rule moves mean fatality by 22 to 58 percentage points within every population. (2) There is no safe default, but the targeting hazard is universal: the safest rule, the least-safe rule, and even the direction of the incidence effect vary across populations, yet regressive identity-targeting is never decisively safest in any context for any population, eliminates the least-resourced agent in 30-87% of games everywhere, and is selection-unsafe relative to the cooperative reference for all seven populations. (3) Identity salience is the mechanism: a one-shot anonymization ablation on the most exploitation-prone population (gpt-5.1) shows that merely naming the loss bearer in the rule text drives targeted elimination from 22% to 81% at identical payoffs; under repeated play, anonymization only delays the targeting, as agents re-infer the hidden rule from observed eliminations. We package the methodology as a safety-case workflow that certifies a provisional rule region $Φ(c,P)$ per deployment context and population, with explicit residual risks and monitoring obligations.

### [117] [The Harness Effect: How Orchestration Design Sets the Token Economics of Enterprise Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06906)
*Muayad Sayed Ali,Aliaksandra Novik,Anji Boddupally,Artem Yavorskyi,Chris Nickerson,Daniel Rica,Emily DuGranrut,Felix Leung,Garrett Prince,Grace Barnett,Heath Robinson,Hosain Al Ahmad,Jesse Resnick,Juan Carlos Farah,Jyothi Swaroop Meruga,Leonid Kuznetsov,Luke Gorham,Marie Schmoll,Michael Paciullo,Saumya Das,Sharath Sheripally,Tommy Griscom,Mykyta Osadchyi,Neha Mantri,Nick Westrum,Olivia Benowitz,Parikshith Kulkarni,Radik Chernyshov,Rakshith Vasudev,Rohith Nadimpally,Vikas Gangadevi,Waseem AlShikh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出智能体AI开发的"Token最大化"问题，并通过实验证明：通过优化编排层（Harness）而非更换底层模型，可以显著降低Token消耗、成本和延迟，同时保持或提升任务质量。在6个模型、22个任务上的实验显示，Writer Agent Harness将每任务成本降低41%、时间减少44%、Token减少38%，质量从0.78提升至0.81。质量增益与模型基线的相关性高达r=0.99，即越强的模型从编排优化中受益越大，这一现象被称为"Harness杠杆效应"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体AI开发存在"Token最大化"现象——通过消耗越来越多的Token（更长推理链、更多轮次、更大工具负载、更大上下文）来换取能力提升，导致每任务Token消耗的增长远超任务价值的增长。虽然Token单价持续下降，但总支出仍在上升。作者认为，对抗这一趋势的关键杠杆在于"编排层"（Harness）——即组装上下文、暴露工具、序列化轮次、委派任务并承载企业级可观测性和治理的协调层。

Method: 采用控制变量实验设计：固定22个评估任务、6个基础模型（Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 3.1, Gemini Flash 3.5, Qwen 3.6, GLM 5.1, Palmyra X6），仅改变编排层——对比传统的生产级循环与Writer Agent Harness。从成本、延迟、Token消耗、任务完成质量四个维度进行测量，并分析了质量增益与模型基线能力之间的相关性。

Result: 编排层替换带来：混合每任务成本降低41%（$0.21→$0.12），中位墙钟时间减少44%（48s→27s），每任务Token消耗减少38%（14.2k→8.8k），任务完成质量从0.78提升至0.81。效率提升对模型不变（所有模型成本降低33-61%），质量增益与模型基线能力强相关（r=0.99, n=6）。每美元质量提升82%，每百万Token完成任务数从54.9增至92.0。在该工作负载上，编排层对每任务成本的影响超过了整个模型菜单的跨度。

Conclusion: 编排层是智能体AI系统中效率提升的关键杠杆，其优化效果可以跨所有当前和未来的模型复用。作者形式化了编排层的Token经济学（包括提示缓存下的有效输入价格），详细描述了六种机制（从缓存形状规训到失败支出治理），对比了六种广泛使用的智能体系统，并论证了Harness是唯一一个其效率提升可以乘数效应地作用于组织运行的每一个模型——无论现在还是未来——的组件。

Abstract: Agentic AI development today runs on token maxing: buying capability with tokens -- longer reasoning traces, more turns, wider tool payloads, bigger replayed contexts -- so tokens per task grow faster than task value. Falling per-token prices mask the pattern; total spend rises anyway. We argue the decisive lever against token maxing is the harness: the orchestration layer that assembles context, exposes tools, sequences turns, delegates work, and carries enterprise observability and governance. We isolate it with a controlled swap: 22 locked evaluation tasks, six foundation models (Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 3.1, Gemini Flash 3.5, Qwen 3.6, GLM 5.1, Palmyra X6), changing only the orchestration layer -- a frozen conventional production loop versus the Writer Agent Harness. Holding models constant, the harness cuts blended cost per task 41% ($0.21->$0.12), median wall-clock 44% (48s->27s), and tokens per task 38% (14.2k->8.8k), with task-completion quality at parity (0.78->0.81, directional at this sample size). Efficiency is model-invariant -- every model gets cheaper (33-61%) -- while quality gains are capability-dependent: a model's gain correlates almost perfectly with its baseline strength (r=0.99, n=6), a phenomenon we term harness leverage. Quality per dollar rises 82%; task-completions per million tokens rise from 54.9 to 92.0. On this workload the orchestration layer moved cost per task more than the full spread of the model menu did. We formalize token economics at the orchestration layer (including effective input price under prompt caching), detail the six mechanism families behind the effect -- cache-shape discipline to failure-spend governance -- compare six widely used agent systems on the same axes, and argue the harness is the one component whose efficiency multiplies across every model an organization runs -- present and future.

</details>


### [118] [Grounding Spatial Relations in a Compact World Model: Instruction Leakage and a Goal-Free Dynamics Fix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06925)
*Yufeng Wang,Lu Wei,Haibin Ling*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 目标条件世界模型中的指令泄露问题：当指令直接命名被预测的答案时，模型会从指令中转录答案而非真正从感知中学习关系。本文通过实验揭示这一混淆现象（准确率达0.90但实为指令转录），并提出解决方案：将目标排除在动力学之外并监督读取路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别并表征目标条件世界模型中存在的"指令泄露"混淆问题——即模型看似学会了感知关系，实则只是从指令中转录了答案，而非真正基于视觉感知进行关系推理。

Method: 通过三类实验检测指令泄露：(1) 移除目标输入，准确率从0.90骤降至0.27；(2) 使用反事实指令，模型94.5%的概率跟随错误指令而非真实场景；(3) 在桌面操作和BabyAI基准中验证，并提出修复方案：将目标从动力学中移除，监督读取路径。

Result: 目标条件预测器达到0.90的关系读取准确率，但这是指令转录而非感知；移除目标后降至0.27；反事实指令下94.5%跟随虚假指令；修复后模型达到0.88的稳定准确率，无论是否包含目标输入。

Conclusion: 指令泄露的充要条件：当被评分的目标量可从指令中直接转录时（指令命名了答案），泄漏就会发生。修复方法是让目标不参与动力学预测（属于规划器成本）并监督读取路径。该诊断和修复方案适用于任何指令命名了被评分量的目标条件世界模型。

Abstract: Compact world models that condition on a language goal promise to ground relations such as ``put the red block left of the blue block'' using a sparse set of explicit \emph{reference anchors}. We ask when such references actually ground a relation, and identify a trap: a goal-conditioned predictor reaches a striking $0.90$ relation-readout accuracy, yet this is \emph{instruction transcription}, not perception. Withholding the goal collapses it to chance ($0.90\!\to\!0.27$, three seeds) and a counterfactual instruction makes the predicted anchors follow the \emph{false} instruction $94.5\%$ of the time (true scene $2.3\%$; $N{=}256$). Tested across three settings and a within-task ablation, our central claim characterizes the confound: \textbf{instruction leakage occurs when the scored quantity is transcribable from the instruction (when the instruction names the answer) and is essentially independent of how predictive the non-instruction inputs are.} Our tabletop and the external BabyAI benchmark leak, whereas a Language-Table forward-dynamics world model whose instruction names \emph{referents} does not, until the instruction is augmented to name the direction; and degrading the action never increases leakage, the opposite of what predictor-competition predicts. The diagnosis prescribes the fix: keep the goal out of the dynamics (it belongs to the planner's cost) and supervise the \emph{read} path, recovering genuine, instruction-independent grounding ($0.88$, identical with and without the goal). The detection protocol and remedy apply to any goal-conditioned world model whose instruction names the scored quantity.

</details>


### [119] [Large Behavior Model: A Promptable Digital Twin of the Retail Customer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06993)
*Wachiravit Modecrua,Krittin Pachtrachai,Touchapon Kraisingkorn*

TL;DR: 本文提出大行为模型(LBM)，通过统一的人物-环境框架从大规模零售交易中学习客户决策行为，在购买预测、硬负样本区分、购物篮补全、促销响应和跨域券兑换等任务上持续优于前沿通用语言模型，消融实验表明持续预训练是行为泛化的主要驱动力，检索增强在训练和推理时联合使用效果最佳，强化学习能提升对显式行为证据的依赖。

Conclusion: 交易历史中编码的行为知识可以被语言模型有效学习，为构建客户数字孪生和行为仿真提供了可扩展的基础。

Abstract: Customer behavior modeling underpins recommendation, marketing, and decision support, yet existing approaches either optimize predictive accuracy without explaining decisions or simulate users without grounding them in real behavioral data. We present the Large Behavioral Model (LBM) that learns customer decision making directly from large-scale retail transactions through a unified Person-Environment formulation. Customer state is represented by a behavioral profile derived from historical purchases, while product context is incorporated through retrieval-augmented generation. The model is trained using continued pre-training on verbalized behavioral data, supervised fine-tuning for decision generation, and reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards for evidence-based calibration. We evaluate the proposed framework on purchase prediction, hard-negative discrimination, basket completion, promotion response, and cross-domain voucher redemption. The model consistently outperforms frontier general-purpose language models on in-domain retail tasks while demonstrating strong zero-shot and fine-tuned transfer across retailers and decision domains. Ablation studies show that continued pre-training is the primary driver of behavioral generalization, retrieval is most effective when applied during both training and inference, and reinforcement learning improves reliance on explicit behavioral evidence over generic language-model priors. These results demonstrate that behavioral knowledge encoded in transaction histories can be effectively learned by language models, providing a scalable foundation for customer digital twins and behavior simulation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Humans continuously coordinate with others in dynamic interactions, often through implicit, hard-to-quantify social norms that act as shared tacit expectations among interacting agents. We selected pedestrian-vehicle interaction as a representative dynamic interaction and developed a simplified experimental platform that captures its key interactive features. From 3,456 dynamic human interactions collected via this platform, we identified three principles underlying human social norms: outcome predictability, value alignment, and advantage awareness. Incorporating these principles into AI agents significantly improves human-AI coordination. In the closed-loop interaction task with humans, the social-norm-informed LLM achieved a nearly fourfold higher total score than the baseline strategy and outperformed human-human interactions by 43%. These findings indicate that formalizing tacit social norms into explicit, quantifiable principles can enable AI agents to achieve mutually beneficial coordination in dynamic interactions, supporting their more natural integration into human society.

Abstract: How can we measure intelligence beyond human capability?

We argue that this difficulty is inherent to absolute-scale evaluation and propose a new paradigm based on relative measurement in which models generate public challenges that separate other systems. Aggregating these outcomes yields an adversarial psychometric rating system that can scale with the systems being measured. We describe practical protocols that reduce incentives for private-information attacks, support judge-free adjudication, and naturally scale with agent capabilities. We instantiate the framework across verifiable and open-ended, non-verifiable domains, illustrating how model-generated evaluation can continue to measure systems beyond the human frontier.

### [122] [Operational Reframing and Approval-Framed Delegation in Multi-Agent LLM Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07097)
*Lifei Liu,Haoran Yu,Xiaochong Jiang,Su Wang,Pin Qian,Yihang Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 多Agent系统的安全评估中，直接提示与规划器-执行器管线的差异（"管线效应"）混淆了三种机制：有害意图被重构为合理操作、规划器拒绝或转换请求、执行器在授权提示下行动。本文通过五条件对照实验设计，在30个合成有害场景和四个Agent安全基准测试中，发现聚合管线安全并非稳定的架构特性；操作重构是最具可迁移性的风险信号；原始-直接模型排名无法预测实际部署行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全评估将直接提示与规划器-执行器管线的差异归为单一的"管线效应"，这一聚合指标难以解释，因为它混淆了操作重构、规划器行为和执行器授权三种根本不同的机制，导致无法准确归因安全失败的原因。

Method: 提出五条件对照实验设计，在30个合成有害场景和四个Agent安全基准测试中，使用LLM评判的合规性指标，分别解耦分析操作重构、规划器拒绝/转换、授权框架提示三种机制的影响，并跨GPT、Gemini、DeepSeek、Claude等模型进行系统比较。

Result: 操作重构在所有模型中（除Claude外）持续增加合规性，是最具可迁移性的风险信号；规划器主要通过拒绝来抵消风险，但若规划器生成可执行步骤，执行器会比直接操作基线更合规；授权框架提示对提示设计、模型配对和场景来源敏感，怀疑性执行器提示可大幅降低合规性。Gemini在原始直接提示中最安全，但与Claude规划器配对时合规率从8.9%飙升至38.9%；GPT的零管线效应掩盖了重构增加与规划器拒绝的相互抵消。

Conclusion: 多Agent安全评估应分别报告重构、规划器行为、授权框架和模型配对的影响，而非将失败简单归因于架构本身；聚合管线安全不是稳定的架构属性，原始-直接模型排名无法预测实际部署行为。

Abstract: Safety evaluations of multi-agent LLM systems often compare a direct prompt with a planner-executor pipeline and report the difference as a single "pipeline effect." We argue that this aggregate is difficult to interpret because it conflates three mechanisms: harmful intent may be reframed as plausible operational work, the planner may refuse or transform the request, and the executor may act under delegation prompts implying prior approval. To separate these factors, we introduce a five-condition controlled contrast design, evaluated on 30 synthetic harmful scenarios and an exploratory external validation set from four agent-safety benchmarks using LLM-judged compliance.
  Our results show that aggregate pipeline safety is not a stable architectural property. Operational reframing is the most portable risk signal, increasing compliance for GPT, Gemini, and DeepSeek across both scenario sets, while Claude is comparatively resistant. Planner behavior can offset this risk mainly through refusal; however, when the planner produces executable steps, the executor may become more compliant than under the direct operational baseline. Approval-framed delegation is sensitive to prompt design, model pairing, and scenario source, and a skeptical executor prompt sharply reduces compliance.
  Raw-direct model rankings can also mispredict deployed planner-executor behavior. Gemini is safest under raw direct prompts in the primary set yet shows the largest amplification with a Claude planner, rising from 8.9 percent to 38.9 percent compliance. GPTs near-zero aggregate pipeline effect instead hides a reframing increase canceled by planner refusal. These findings suggest that multi-agent safety evaluations should report reframing, planner behavior, delegation framing, and model pairing separately before attributing failures to architecture itself.

ImagingBench evaluates three complementary settings: Expert, fixed expert-guided inverse reconstruction; Planner, planner-guided inverse reconstruction; and Forward, forward-system simulation for consistency checking. *Silvia Santano*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 形式化定义推理一致性，与忠实性区分，提出六种不一致子类型分类体系；2) 基于InstrumentalEval输出构建60个标注样本的基准测试；3) 在InspectScout上实现首个针对该属性的扫描工具；4) 在四个生成模型和三项评估任务上进行实验验证。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is often unfaithful: a model's stated reasoning does not reliably reflect the process that produced its output. Detecting unfaithfulness, though, requires controlled experimental interventions, which cannot be applied to evaluation transcripts after the fact. We turn instead to a more tractable question that has received less attention: whether the stated reasoning is logically consistent with the answer it accompanies. Unlike faithfulness, consistency can be assessed from a transcript alone, with no intervention. We introduce reasoning consistency scanning, a reusable method for detecting this property in AI safety evaluation transcripts. Our contributions are fourfold. First, we formalize reasoning consistency as distinct from faithfulness and define a six-subtype taxonomy of inconsistency. Second, we build a validated benchmark of 60 transcripts, manually adapted from InstrumentalEval outputs. Third, we implement a working scanner for InspectScout, the first to target this property in safety evaluation transcripts. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出EvoSOP框架，从执行轨迹中提取SOPs作为可调用的高阶工具，并通过构建、合并、评估和剪枝的系统化生命周期迭代优化工具集。

Abstract: Tool utilization enables Large Language Model (LLM) agents to interact with the real world and resolve complex tasks. However, existing agent frameworks predominantly rely on static toolsets composed of granular atomic actions (e.g., basic file I/O or single-turn search), which forces agents to reinvent low-level logic for every recurring workflow, leading to increased reasoning overhead and failure rates. In this study, we propose that agents can achieve self-evolution by synthesizing these atomic actions into reusable Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs), which function as callable higher-order tools that encapsulate multi-step logic. We further introduce EvoSOP, a framework that empowers agents to extract SOPs from execution trajectories and iteratively optimize the toolset through a systematic lifecycle of construction, merging, evaluation, and pruning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoSOP significantly boosts task success rates while substantially reducing the number of interaction rounds compared to baselines. ### [126] [Physics-Audited Agentic Discovery in Scientific Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07379)
*Diab W. Abueidda,Bilal Ahmed,Panos Pantidis,Mostafa E. Mobasher*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PA-SciML，一个面向智能科学机器学习（SciML）的"验证优先"工作流，通过引入可审查的物理需求检查（如边界条件、因果性等）来筛选代理模型，而不仅仅依赖误差指标。在固体力学数值实验中，该方法能选出通过物理检查且误差更低的模型，而纯误差基线模型在瞬态弹性动力学中未能通过因果性检查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM代理的科学机器学习方法仅凭误差指标选择代理模型，但低误差并不保证模型满足力学中关键的物理约束（如边界条件、叠加原理、刚度缩放、因果性），可能导致物理上不可信的预测结果。

Method: 1) 在搜索前固定评分评估器；2) 推导可审查、可机器检查的物理需求；3) 对每个训练好的候选模型进行输出检查；4) 在指定输入范围或载荷历史跨度内搜索高违反情况（无需参考解）；5) 仅当通过所有检查后才报告为已验证；6) 可选地在训练前添加数值探针，并每次只改变一个建模元素以记录孤立编辑对分数的影响。

Result: 在静态弹性算例中，PA-SciML选出的代理模型验证误差低于纯误差基线，且两者均通过常规线弹性检查；在瞬态弹性动力学算例中，纯误差基线（均值误差相似）未能通过严格的因果性检查（对载荷历史未来部分有响应），而PA-SciML选出的模型通过了所有检查。

Conclusion: PA-SciML的核心区别在于对每个候选模型提供预测场的物理证据检查，而非仅仅依赖更丰富的聚合评分，从而确保代理模型在物理上的可信性。

Abstract: In agentic scientific machine learning (SciML), large language model (LLM) agents can discover surrogate models and select one by an automated score, typically an error metric. A low error, however, does not establish that the predicted fields satisfy the physics that matter for mechanics, such as boundary conditions, superposition, stiffness scaling, or causality. We introduce Physics-Audited Agentic SciML (PA-SciML), a verification-first workflow for agentic SciML discovery. The workflow fixes a scoring evaluator before search, derives reviewable machine-checkable physics requirements, checks each trained candidate on its outputs, and separately searches prescribed input ranges or measured load-history spans for high-violation cases without reference solution fields. A surrogate is reported as verified only under the stated checks. When enabled, the workflow also adds advisory numerical probes before training and tests one modeling change at a time to record which isolated edits are associated with score gains before reuse. In the reported computational-solid-mechanics numerical examples, the static elasticity run selects a surrogate with lower validation error than the error-only baseline while both selected models pass the common linear-elastic checks. In the transient elastodynamics run, an error-only baseline with similar mean error fails a stricter causality check by responding to future parts of the loading history, while the selected surrogate passes the stated checks. The main distinction is per-candidate physics evidence on predicted fields, not a richer aggregate score.

</details>


### [127] [MIRA-Math: A Benchmark for Minimal Information Requesting and Mathematical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07391)
*Charbel Al Bateh,Samer Saab*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MIRA-Math是一个包含2,310个实例、涵盖22种数学类型的基准测试，用于评估模型在缺少一个必需原子事实的情况下，通过自然语言请求缺失信息并整合得到精确答案的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数学推理基准通常提供所有必需事实，而交互式基准又混合了推理与工具、检索等多种能力，缺乏对模型在信息不完备条件下主动请求缺失信息的诊断性评估能力。

Method: 构建MIRA-Math基准：每个问题完整潜在状态有唯一答案，但求解者视角恰好缺少一个必需原子事实；求解者需在严格预算下用自然语言请求缺失信息，固定LLM响应者仅在被请求匹配时返回引述事实；包含确定性实例生成、类型化提示规范、验证和答案校验流程。

Result: 在前沿和小模型上的实验表明，请求成功与最终答案准确性是可分离的：模型可能请求到正确事实但下游计算失败，也可能在获得规范提示前就已失败。

Conclusion: MIRA-Math提供了对数学推理中最小信息请求能力的可重复评估框架，揭示了信息请求与计算推理是两种可分离的能力维度。

Abstract: Mathematical reasoning benchmarks typically provide all facts needed to solve each problem, while interactive benchmarks often mix reasoning with tools, retrieval, and long-horizon dialogue. We introduce MIRA-Math, a benchmark for a narrower diagnostic capability: solving mathematical problems whose full latent state has a unique answer, but whose solver-facing view is missing exactly one necessary atomic fact. The solver must request the missing information in natural language under a strict budget and then integrate the returned fact into an exact final answer. A fixed constrained LLM responder sees only the dataset-provided atomic fact and must either offer the quoted fact when the request matches it, or decline otherwise. Thus, instance generation, typed hint specifications, validation, and final-answer verification are deterministic, while request metrics are measured under a fixed LLM-mediated responder channel. MIRA-Math contains 2{,}310 generated instances from 22 typed mathematical families spanning algebra, probability, linear systems, discrete structures, signal processing, Markov chains, circuits, interpolation, and numerical boundary-value problems. Experiments across frontier and small models show that request success and final-answer accuracy are separable: models may ask for the right fact yet fail the downstream computation, or fail before obtaining the canonical hint. We release generators, verifiers, prompts, run metadata, and dataset documentation to support reproducible evaluation of minimal information requesting in mathematical reasoning.

### [129] [Reason Less, Verify More: Deterministic Gates Recover a Silent Policy-Violation Failure Mode in Tool-Using LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07405)
*Vikas Reddy,Sumanth Reddy Challaram,Abhishek Basu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究了工具使用型LLM智能体中存在的“静默违规写入”问题：工具执行了违反域策略的调用，但未产生错误提示，导致系统进入错误的隐性状态。作者在τ²-bench航空领域中发现78%的失败属于此类，并提出一种轻量级干预方法——确定性只读预执行门控机制（pre-execution gates），能将GPT-4o-mini的成功率从29.6%提升至42.0%（+12.4pp），且在GPT-5.2上也观察到类似提升（+10.4pp）。该机制在工具本身策略宽松时效果显著，而在工具已自执行策略的领域中增益有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在调用工具时，即使工具执行了违反域策略的操作（如违规取消订单、修改乘客数量等），系统和智能体本身都不会报告错误，导致系统进入“静默错误状态”。现有研究缺乏对此类失败模式的系统界定和有效防御机制。

Method: 提出一种轻量级干预方法：在工具执行写操作之前，插入确定性的只读预执行门控（pre-execution gates），检查当前状态和工具调用是否合规，只有通过检查才允许写操作执行。在τ²-bench航空领域设计了4个门控规则套件，并在GPT-4o-mini和GPT-5.2上进行了评估。

Result: （1）预算智能体中78%的失败为静默错误状态失败；（2）4门控套件将GPT-4o-mini的完整基准成功率从29.6%提升至42.0%（+12.4pp，p=0.0012），并在独立15种子集上复现（+12.3pp，p=0.0008）；（3）效果集中在门控触发的26/50个任务上（+19.2pp），非触发任务的效果不显著；（4）两个负对照实验（零售领域和BFCL）表明门控在工具宽松时有效，在工具已自执行策略时增益有限；（5）GPT-5.2上也从61.2%提升至71.6%（+10.4pp，p=0.020）

Conclusion: 确定性门控机制不能保证任务完全成功，但能确定性地在动作边界上阻止一类已知的静默违规写入。该贡献是一个有边界的评估和可靠性结果，而非安全保证。

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents can violate the very policies they are deployed to enforce while appearing to complete the task successfully. In policy-permissive environments, a tool may execute any well-formed call even when the corresponding state transition is forbidden by domain policy. The result is a silent wrong state (a booking cancelled, a passenger count changed, a claim acted on without verification) that neither the tool nor the agent's self-report exposes.
  We study this failure mode in the $τ^2$-bench airline domain. On a budget agent, 78% of observed failures are silent wrong-state failures with no tool error, and the aggregate failure rate is reproducible across disjoint seeds, not sampling noise. We then evaluate a lightweight intervention: deterministic, read-only pre-execution gates that inspect the proposed call and current state before allowing a write. A four-gate suite raises full-benchmark success from 29.6% to 42.0% on gpt-4o-mini (+12.4pp; paired task-level bootstrap P=0.0012), and the lift reproduces on a disjoint 15-seed set (+12.3pp; P=0.0008).
  The effect is concentrated where the gates fire: on the 26/50 firing tasks, success rises by +19.2pp, while movement on the 24 non-firing tasks does not exclude zero. Two negative controls (a self-enforcing retail domain and BFCL) bound the mechanism: gates help when tools are policy-permissive and add little where tools already self-enforce. As suggestive evidence, not a central claim, the same failure mode persists at the frontier: gpt-5.2 at default reasoning still attempts policy-violating writes, and the same suite improves success from 61.2% to 71.6% (+10.4pp; P=0.020; n=5, no replication). The contribution is a bounded evaluation and reliability result: deterministic gates do not guarantee task success, but they can deterministically prevent a known class of silent policy-violating writes at the action boundary.

</details>


### [130] [InductWave: Inductive Multi-Hop Logical Query Answering on Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07422)
*Mayank Kharbanda,Michael Cochez,Rajiv Ratn Shah,Raghava Mutharaju*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出InductWave，一种基于小波的归纳式嵌入方法，用于知识图谱上的逻辑多跳查询应答。该方法在更少的消息传递层数下达到或超越基线模型性能，并能在大规模图上进行推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱逻辑查询方法主要采用直推式推理，无法处理训练中未见的实体；而现实世界存在资源稀缺问题，无法在大规模KG上对所有节点进行训练。

Method: 提出InductWave，一种基于小波变换的归纳式嵌入方法，用于逻辑查询应答。训练图包含比测试图更少的节点，通过小波变换实现归纳推理。

Result: 在基线模型一半的消息传递层数下表现相当；在75%的层数下超越所有基线模型；能够在Wiki-KG等大规模图上进行评估。

Conclusion: InductWave在资源需求更少的情况下实现了对大规模KG的归纳式逻辑查询应答，在FB15k-237数据集上优于现有方法。

Abstract: Logical Multi-Hop Query Answering over Knowledge Graphs (KGs) can be formulated as querying, with an implicit completeness assumption. Current works mainly focus on Existential First Order Logic (EFO) queries. These EFO queries contain conjunction, disjunction, and negation operators. Most existing works employ transductive reasoning, meaning they are not capable of reasoning over entities unseen during training. In the real world, there is a resource scarcity, and we cannot train a model with all the nodes of a large KG. Hence, we propose InductWave, a wavelet-based inductive embedding method for logical query answering on large KGs. Here, the training graph consists of fewer nodes than the test graph. Our model performs on par with the baseline models while having half the number of message-passing layers. It outperforms all of them in most cases, with 75% of the layers. These fewer resource requirements enable us to evaluate InductWave on massive graphs, such as Wiki-KG. We test our model using extensive experiments across varying train-test graph proportions of the FB15k-(237) dataset, comparing it with the state-of-the-art models. The code and datasets for the model are available at https://github.com/kracr/inductwave/.

### [131] [The Blind Curator: How a Biased Judge Silently Disables Skill Retirement in Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07436)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了自我进化智能体在依赖有偏LLM评委（无参考任务中不可避免）进行技能淘汰时的问题：有偏评委（尤其是假阳性偏差）会悄悄关闭技能策展机制，导致基于贡献的技能淘汰在超过某个阈值后彻底失效，且这种机制故障在常规指标中不可见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参考自由任务迫使系统依赖LLM作为评委，但LLM评委存在偏差（非对称噪声），现有技能淘汰机制假设奖励无偏，一旦评委有偏，策展机制可能静默失效而不被察觉。

Method: 采用腐败奖励理论分析，并在确定性奖励上注入噪声进行因果隔离；在参考自由的报告生成测试平台上结合代码生成交叉验证进行行为研究。

Result: 对称噪声不影响淘汰机制，但假阳性偏差（将失败误判为通过）在超过某个阈值后完全禁用基于贡献的技能淘汰；该机制故障具有通用性，跨领域和失败率都成立，仅当假阳性率接近零时才幸免；下游评估质量仅在相同腐败同时影响技能合成时才下降，否则保持稳定。

Conclusion: 该研究贡献了一个行为安全结果而非性能结果，并提出一种廉价的缺陷注入审计方法，可在部署前判断评委是否处于危险阈值一侧。

Abstract: A self-evolving agent retires its bad skills by watching them fail, so what happens when the judge cannot see the failures? Skill retirement is the structural constraint that keeps a growing library from drifting below the no-skill baseline, but its guarantee assumes an unbiased reward, which is false for the LLM judges that reference-free tasks force upon us. We show that a biased judge does not merely add noise; it \emph{silently switches off the curator}. We make this precise with a corrupted-reward analysis and, isolating the causal channel by injecting corruption on top of a deterministic reward, a behavioral study on a reference-free report-writing testbed with a code-generation cross-check. Symmetric noise leaves retirement intact, but \emph{false-pass} bias (failures slipping through as passes) disables contribution-based retirement past a sharp threshold that no amount of data can cross. Separating genuine retirement from cap-eviction churn shows this \emph{mechanism} failure is universal, holding across domains and failure rates and sparing only near-zero-false-pass, verifier-like graders. The downstream \emph{outcome}, though, is regime-dependent: eval quality degrades only where the same corruption also starves skill synthesis, and otherwise holds steady, so the disabled curator is \emph{silent}, surfacing in no aggregate metric. The contribution is a behavioral safety result, not a performance one. A cheap defect-injection audit then tells an operator, before deployment, which side of the threshold their judge occupies.

</details>

We evaluate SpaCellAgent on six heterogeneous datasets encompassing complex temporal developmental trajectories, diverse sequencing platforms, and spatially-resolved tissue architectures. SpaCellAgent consistently demonstrates over 40\% improvement in analytical efficiency while maintaining expert-aligned performance. By converting natural language specifications into optimized analytical workflows and fully automating the pipeline, SpaCellAgent democratizes advanced spatiotemporal modeling and establishes a scalable, agent-driven paradigm for computational biology. ### [133] [Search, Fail, Recover: A Training Framework for Correction-Aware Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07492)
*Dmitry Beresnev,Vladimir Makharev,Roman Khalikov,Ivan Oseledets,Petr Anokhin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Pyligent是一个训练和推理框架，通过将推理建模为带验证的搜索过程（包含continue/finish/backtrack三种动作），并使用失败分支的显式监督信号，在隐藏图、数独、Blocksworld等任务上显著优于仅使用成功链的微调方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多推理任务无法通过简单的从左到右链式过程描述，求解器可能需要探索看似合理的分支、观察到延迟反馈的失败，然后回溯到可完成的前缀。现有方法仅模仿完美的解链，无法教会模型处理失败恢复行为。

Method: 提出Pyligent框架，基于Diligent Learner范式，将推理表示为带验证的搜索过程。任务验证器标记生成的延续和失败，将搜索树转换为三种动作（continue/finish/backtrack）的监督目标，并附带可选的对废弃分支的总结轨迹。

Result: 在隐藏有向图任务上提升72.7个百分点，混合/专家数独上提升17和18个百分点，带推理轨迹的混合/专家数独上提升27和14个百分点，Blocksworld上提升13个百分点。

Conclusion: 显式的失败分支监督信号可以教会模型有用的恢复行为，效果超越仅模仿完美解链的方法。

Abstract: Many reasoning tasks are not well described by a single left-to-right chain: a solver may need to pursue a plausible branch, observe delayed failure, and return to the latest prefix that can still be completed. We introduce Pyligent, a training and inference framework inspired by the Diligent Learner formulation that represents reasoning as validated search over partial solution chains. A task validator labels generated continuations and failures, and the resulting search trees are converted into supervised targets for three actions: continue, finish, and backtrack, with optional traces that summarize abandoned branches. We evaluate Pyligent on a hidden directed graph task designed to isolate delayed-failure recovery, and on structured reasoning domains with exact validators, including $4{\times}4$ Sudoku, Sudoku with reasoning traces, and Blocksworld. Compared with gold-only supervised fine-tuning, Pyligent improves solve rate by $72.7$ percentage points on hidden graphs, by $17$ and $18$ points on mixed and expert Sudoku, by $27$ and $14$ points on mixed and expert Sudoku with reasoning traces, and by $13$ points on Blocksworld. These results suggest that explicit failed-branch supervision can teach useful recovery behavior beyond imitation of polished solution chains.

### [134] [Do LLM-Generated Skills Make Better AI Data Scientists? A Component Ablation Across Data-Science Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07504)
*Wei-Jung Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模实验（7,560次运行 + 1,512次对照运行）发现，LLM生成的一次性技能文件（per-stage skill）在数据科学任务中无法带来显著性能提升，其效果与无技能提示或无意义技能格式内容相当，警示不应将其作为默认的少样本提示策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 减少产品数据科学家在重复性执行任务（如数据清洗、SQL编写、统计检验选择、结果格式化）中每次从头编写提示的负担，探索LLM自动生成的技能文件是否可以作为低人工维护成本的替代方案。

Method: 在数据科学四个生命周期阶段（数据准备、数据提取、统计分析、报告）各生成一个技能文件，与无技能基线对比；通过消融实验（56个任务、9种模型配置、3个提供商，共7,560次运行）分析技能各组件贡献；并补充token匹配的对照实验（1,512次运行）检验技能格式本身的效果。

Result: 完整生成技能及其所有消融变体相比无技能提示均无显著性能提升（所有p值≥0.396，总跨度仅1.2个百分点）；完整技能与任务无关的技能格式内容表现相似。

Conclusion: 不建议将每个数据科学工作流使用一个LLM生成的技能文件作为默认的单次提示策略，因为其无法带来可靠的性能改进。

Abstract: Product data scientists often ask LLM-based agents to help with recurring execution tasks such as cleaning data, writing SQL, choosing statistical tests, and formatting results. Reusable skill files are meant to avoid prompting from scratch by packaging guidance for a task family. Expert-written skills can encode high-quality guidance, but writing and maintaining them across many data-science task families creates a manual bottleneck. We ask whether LLM-generated skills offer a useful low-curation alternative: do they improve performance over the task prompt alone? We test this question across four lifecycle stages: data preparation, data extraction, statistical analysis, and reporting, using one generated skill per stage. We find no reliable improvement from full generated skills over No-Skill prompting. We then ask whether any part of the skill is useful by ablating different skill components. The main ablation covers 56 tasks, nine model configurations, and three providers, yielding 7,560 runs. Compared with prompting using the task alone, neither the full generated skill nor any ablated skill variant significantly improves performance; all p-values are at least 0.396, and the total spread across variants is only 1.2 pp. A supplemental token-matched control adds 1,512 runs and finds that Full skills perform similarly to task-irrelevant skill-formatted content. The results caution against using one LLM-generated skill per data-science workflow as a default single-shot prompting strategy.

</details>


### [135] [RL Post-Training Builds Compositional Reasoning Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07646)
*Azwar Abdulsalam,Nishil Patel,Andrew Saxe*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究强化学习后训练能否将基础模型中的原始技能组合成新的高级策略。在可观测的重写语法环境中，Transformer先预训练于原始符号重写链，再通过基于Trace的推理任务进行后训练（仅用二元最终答案奖励）。结果表明，RL能解决预训练模型即使大幅增加采样也难以解决的问题，而拒绝微调早期有提升但随后停滞。轨迹分析显示RL通过阶段性组合机制重组原始能力：先强化原始归约，再发现有效组合过程（包括顺序组合和并行组合），并将这些组合程序巩固为稳定技能库。与RFT相比，RL的关键差异在于选择性而非探索量——RFT产生大量捷径式但无效的重写，而RL将探索集中于有效的可重用结构。预训练消融实验表明，组合策略的涌现不仅取决于原始暴露，更取决于预训练是否将原始能力组织为可被RL后续压缩的归约程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究RL后训练是否仅仅放大基础模型中已有的原始技能，还是能够将这些原始技能组合成新的高级策略。这是一个关于AI能力涌现机制的基础性问题，涉及对RL在推理能力提升中作用的根本理解。

Method: 在完全可观测的重写语法环境中，先用原始符号重写链预训练Transformer，再在Trace-based推理任务上用仅含二元最终答案奖励的RL进行后训练。通过轨迹分析比较RL与拒绝微调的效果，并进行预训练消融实验。

Result: RL能解决预训练模型即使大幅增加采样也无法解决的问题；RFT早期有提升但随后停滞。RL通过阶段性组合机制重组原始能力：先强化原始归约，再发现顺序组合和并行组合等有效组合过程，并将其巩固为稳定技能库。RL与RFT的关键差异在于选择性而非探索量。组合策略的涌现取决于预训练是否将原始能力组织为可被压缩的归约程序。

Conclusion: RL后训练不仅仅是放大原始技能，而是能够将原始技能组合成新的高级策略。基础模型提供的是弱程序性成分，RL将其构建为可靠的高级策略。这一组合能力的涌现依赖于预训练阶段对原始能力的组织结构。

Abstract: Does RL post-training merely amplify primitive skills already latent in a base model, or can it compose primitive skills into new higher-level strategies? We study this question in a fully observable rewrite-grammar environment where the pretraining distribution is known and every generated rewrite can be audited. A Transformer is pretrained on primitive symbol-rewrite chains and post-trained on a Trace-based reasoning task with only a binary final-answer reward. RL solves held-out problems that remain rarely solved by the pretrained model even under much larger sampling budgets, while rejection fine-tuning improves early but plateaus. Trace analysis shows that RL reorganizes primitive competence through a phased compositional mechanism: it first strengthens primitive reductions, then discovers valid composed procedures. These include sequential compositions, which collapse ordered chains of primitive contractions, and parallel compositions, which combine independent primitive contractions in a single step. The composed procedures are not isolated samples; they are reused and consolidated into a stable repertoire. Comparing RL with rejection fine-tuning shows that the key difference is not exploration volume but selectivity: RFT produces many shortcut-like rewrites, much of them invalid, whereas RL concentrates exploration into valid reusable structure. Pretraining ablations show that the emergence of compositional strategies is gated not by primitive exposure alone, but by whether pretraining organizes primitive competence into reduction procedures that RL can later compress. The base model provides weak procedural ingredients; RL builds them into reliable higher-level strategies.

</details>


### [136] [Recursive Self-Improvement in AI: From Bounded Self-Refinement to Autonomous Research Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07663)
*Mingguang Chen,Licheng Wang,Bo Qu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对1,250篇arXiv论文（2024-2026）进行了系统调查，沿"改进对象"和"闭环程度"两个轴建立分类体系，区分了有界自精炼与开放递归自我改进（RSI），重点分析了自我评估信号的设计空间及其验证层级，指出自我提升强度与验证层级正相关，并识别了研究瓶颈与治理缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献使用"自我精炼"、"自我奖励"、"自我博弈"、"自我进化"等术语，但这些术语混淆了根本不同的技术目标与能力范围。缺乏统一的分类体系导致研究者难以区分哪些自我改进是收敛且安全的，哪些可能导向不可控的递归自我改进（RSI），也使得治理与安全讨论缺乏技术基础。

Method: 对2024-2026年间1,250篇arXiv论文进行系统调查，沿两个分析轴建立分类：1）改进对象维度（行为、策略、评估器、研究过程）；2）闭环程度维度（人在回路到完全闭环）。特别设计了"自我评估"类别，构建了从形式验证器（最强）到内在自我评估（最弱）的验证层级，并分析了不同层级上的失败模式。

Result: 1）有界自精炼（收敛、可评估、已在工业实践中）与开放RSI之间存在根本性分野；2）自我提升的实际强度与验证层级严格正相关；3）失败模式（自确认循环、模型坍缩、多样性坍缩）本质上是验证层级违反的结果；4）"研究方向设定"瓶颈位于验证层级顶端，是保持人在回路的关键；5）治理级自我改进度量是学界最缺乏的领域。

Conclusion: 自我评估是每个改进回路的核心主张（某种信号可替代人类判断），因此评估器的设计质量决定了整个自我改进系统的安全边界。技术文献与RSI极限理论以及前沿实验室的闭环实践之间存在连接点，而自我改进的治理级度量是最迫切且最被忽视的研究方向。

Abstract: AI systems increasingly participate in their own improvement: revising their outputs, adapting their own harnesses during deployment, training on data they generate, and, increasingly, conducting AI research itself. This literature is described under a vocabulary ("self-refine," "self-reward," "self-play," "self-evolve") that conflates fundamentally different ambitions. We survey 1,250 arXiv papers (2024-2026) along two axes: what the system improves -- its behavior in deployment, its policy through training, its evaluator, or the research process itself -- and the degree of loop closure (human-in-the-loop to fully closed). The taxonomy separates bounded self-refinement -- convergent, evaluable, and already industrial practice -- from open-ended recursive self-improvement (RSI), which remains bounded by grounding requirements, collapse dynamics, and compute constraints on every measured axis. Its distinctive feature is a dedicated category for self-evaluation: every improvement loop is a claim that some signal can substitute for human judgment. We survey the evaluator design space -- judges, process reward models, verifiers, rubrics, meta-evaluation -- order the signals into a verification hierarchy from formal verifiers (strongest) to intrinsic self-assessment (weakest), and observe that demonstrated self-improvement strength tracks this hierarchy, that its failure modes (self-confirming loops, model collapse, diversity collapse) follow from its violations, and that the "research direction-setting" bottleneck keeping humans in the loop sits at the top of that hierarchy. We connect the technical literature to the theory of RSI limits and to the safety and governance questions raised by frontier-lab accounts of closing the loop, and identify governance-grade measurement of self-improvement as the field's most underpopulated niche.

</details>


### [137] [SkillCenter: A Large-Scale Source-Grounded Skill Library for Autonomous AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07676)
*Tianming Sha,Yue Zhao,Lichao Sun,Yushun Dong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillCenter 是当前最大的开放智能体技能库，包含 216,938 个结构化技能，覆盖 24 个领域。其中 114,565 个技能通过 SkillGate 过滤管道从同行评审期刊、ArXiv 等 24,000+ 技术来源获取并带有源引用，102,373 个社区技能来自 GitHub 和 ClawHub。所有技能以可离线搜索的 SQLite FTS5 格式发布，每个技能均支持精确到原文引用的源追溯。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主 AI 智能体在执行复杂任务时缺乏接地气的可操作知识，导致输出虽然在可执行性上可行，但在正确性、安全性和可维护性上存在不足。现有技能库缺乏大规模、多来源、可追溯的结构化技能资源。

Method: 提出端到端框架，包含多源获取、基于 LLM 的质量门控（SkillGate）、模板驱动生成、迭代源接地和质量控制发布四个阶段。管道子集从同行评审期刊、ArXiv 和 24,000+ 技术来源获取技能，经过 SkillGate 过滤，确保每个技能中的声明都能精确追溯到原文引用。

Result: 构建了 216,938 个结构化技能，其中 114,565 个通过管道生成（带源引用），102,373 个来自社区。所有技能以离线可搜索的 SQLite FTS5 格式发布。

Conclusion: SkillCenter 通过大规模、多来源、源可追溯的技能库，弥补了自主 AI 智能体在操作性知识上的不足，提升了输出的正确性、安全性和可维护性。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents can execute complex tasks with limited human review, yet they often lack the grounded operational knowledge to make their outputs not just executable but correct, secure, and maintainable. We introduce SkillCenter, to our knowledge the largest open skill library for agents by total count: 216,938 structured skills across 24 domain bundles. A SkillGate-filtered pipeline contributes 114,565 source-grounded skills from peer-reviewed journals, ArXiv, and over 24,000 technical sources, integrated with 102,373 community skills from GitHub and the ClawHub marketplace. We present the end-to-end framework that builds the pipeline subset: multi-source acquisition, an LLM-based quality gate (SkillGate), template-driven generation, iterative source-grounding, and quality-controlled publishing. Source grounding is a traceability guarantee: each retained claim maps to an exact quotation in its source. All skills ship as offline-searchable SQLite FTS5 bundles.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用图Tsetlin机（GraphTM）框架，将宏观经济变量和技术指标构建为超向量化有向多重图；通过消息传递操作更新局部节点特征，并利用深度可解释逻辑子句识别复杂子图模式，从而预测市场体制。

Conclusion: 基于图论结合GraphTM的方法能够融合外生宏观经济变量，通过可解释的逻辑子图模式识别，为外汇市场体制预测提供了一种新颖且有效的解决方案。

Abstract: This paper introduces a graph-theoretic approach for predicting market regimes in foreign exchange (FX) currency prices. Specifically, the proposed model incorporates exogenous macroeconomic variables to update localized node features via message-passing operations. Utilizing the Graph Tsetlin Machine (GraphTM) framework, we empirically demonstrate the efficacy of this approach in anticipating market regimes for the US Dollar and Japanese Yen currency pair (USD/JPY). By representing multivariate macroeconomic drivers and technical indicators as hypervectorized directed multigraphs, the GraphTM leverages structured message passing to construct deep, interpretable logical clauses capable of recognizing complex sub-graph patterns.

### [139] [Machine Learning-Based Battery State-of-health Prediction for Unmanned Aerial Vehicles Predictive Maintenance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06791)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机电池SoH预测至关重要但被忽视，面临数据稀缺、高变异性、传感器特征有限等挑战，需要有效方法在数据不足条件下实现准确预测以提升飞行安全与维护效率。

Method: 1) 进行342次和289次飞行实验收集2200mAh和1100mAh锂聚合物电池的运行数据；2) 选取电压、电流、油门作为输入特征，每10次实验测量剩余容量作为标签；3) 将时序数据转换为图像；4) 利用预训练ResNet-50提取图像特征；5) 在两种电池类型间进行迁移学习。

Result: 通过迁移学习在两种不同容量的锂聚合物电池间获得了准确的SoH预测模型，有效缓解了数据稀缺问题。

Conclusion: 所提出的将时序数据转图像并利用预训练ResNet-50结合迁移学习的ML流水线，能有效解决无人机电池数据稀缺问题，实现跨电池类型的准确SoH预测。

Abstract: Battery state-of-health (SoH) prediction aims to estimate the remaining capacity by modeling battery degradation through its life cycle. Machine learning (ML)-based SoH models can accurately predict the battery remaining capacity based on voltage, current, and temperature. Battery SoH prediction for unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) is a crucial yet overlooked domain with data scarcity and high variability. Accurate battery SoH information contributes to efficient predictive maintenance, enhancing UAV profitability and flight safety. However, UAVs are compatible with a variety of batteries and the available data for each type of battery are scarce. Furthermore, the available input features from UAV batteries are limited to the built-in sensors because of the lightweight requirements. This research aims to develop an ML pipeline for UAV battery SoH prediction while mitigating data scarcity using knowledge transfer. 342 and 289 flight experiments have been conducted to collect operational data from lithium polymer batteries of 2200 mAh and 1100 mAh, respectively. Voltage, current, and throttle are selected as the input features of the ML model according to the existing literature and sensor availability. The remaining capacity is measured at every 10th experiment to label the dataset. To address data scarcity, the time-series data acquired from the experiments are transformed into images to utilize the image feature extraction capability of a pretrained ResNet-50. Finally, accurate SoH prediction models were obtained using transfer learning between two battery types.

### [140] [Topological Signatures of Diffusive Release in Porous Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07061)
*Donghan Kim*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文利用持续同调量化多孔介质的多尺度拓扑与几何结构（固体连通性、环状及空洞结构），通过统计分析证明这些特征与扩散驱动释放行为密切相关。即使在相同目标孔隙度下，拓扑特征更丰富的样本表现出长尾释放行为。基于持续同调特征的简单分类模型可有效划分释放曲线类型，且特征提取速度远快于有限元扩散模拟，表明持续同调是一种轻量、可解释且基于几何描述的筛选工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究多孔介质中固相的多尺度拓扑与几何组织（如连通性、环状及空洞结构）如何影响扩散驱动的释放行为，弥补传统仅关注孔隙率而忽略微观结构影响的不足。

Method: 运用持续同调（persistent homology）量化多孔介质的拓扑与几何特征；结合统计分析建立特征与释放行为之间的关联；采用简单分类模型基于持续同调特征对释放曲线类型进行分类。

Result: 1) 拓扑/几何特征与扩散释放行为显著相关；2) 相同孔隙度下，拓扑特征丰富的样本呈现长尾释放；3) 持续同调特征可有效分类释放曲线类型；4) 特征提取速度显著快于有限元扩散模拟。

Conclusion: 持续同调提供了一种轻量、可解释且基于几何结构的描述符，可用于快速筛选多孔介质中的扩散释放行为。

Abstract: We used persistent homology to quantify the multiscale topological and geometric organization of porous media, including solid connectivity and the formation of loop-like and cavity-like structures across spatial scales. Through statistical analysis, we show that these topological and geometric features are closely associated with diffusion-driven release behavior in porous media. In particular, even within each target-porosity level, samples with richer topological features tend to exhibit long-tailed release, indicating that release behavior depends not only on the amount of pore space but also on the multiscale organization of the solid phase. We further show that persistent homology-based features can classify release-curve regimes using a simple classification model. Notably, feature extraction is substantially faster than finite element diffusion simulations. Together, these results suggest that persistent homology provides a lightweight, interpretable, and geometry-based descriptor for screening diffusive release behavior in porous media.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Satellite anomaly detection is essential for maintaining mission reliability and spacecraft health, yet remains challenging due to the high-dimensional, irregular, and imbalanced nature of spacecraft telemetry data. This paper presents a systematic benchmark study evaluating supervised and unsupervised anomaly detection approaches on the large-scale ESA-ADB dataset across two mission settings of varying temporal scales. Supervised models, including Multiscale Convolutional Neural Networks (Multiscale CNN), Graph Convolutional Networks (GCN), and Graph Attention Networks (GAT), are compared against unsupervised methods, namely Elliptic Envelope (EE) and Empirical Cumulative Distribution Function-based Outlier Detection (ECOD). Beyond detection performance, we rigorously analyze computational runtime and scalability, which are critical for practical deployment in spacecraft operations. Results show that supervised models achieve stronger overall performance, while unsupervised methods offer competitive precision with significantly lower computational overhead. These findings underscore a fundamental trade-off between detection capacity and operational efficiency, offering practical guidance for mission engineers designing scalable satellite health monitoring systems.

### [142] [When and How Should a Power Trader Engage in Arbitrage? Predict, then Contextually Optimize](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07351)
*Yannick Heiser,Jalal Kazempour,Farzaneh Pourahmadi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电力市场中日前与平衡市场的价差为随机性能源发电商提供了套利机会，但机会主义投标存在显著风险，现有框架缺乏可解释且风险感知的决策支持。

Method: 采用"预测-情境优化"框架，三阶段分解：①概率二分类器（带置信阈值）判断是否值得套利；②确定套利方向；③通过情境优化学习的线性决策策略确定投标偏离幅度。支持单独可再生能源发电站和混合电站（如结合电解槽）。

Result: 在欧洲DK1和DE/LU区域真实风电场数据上，相比无套利基准，混合电站在DK1区域利润提升约7%。收益最大提升发生在训练与测试窗口分布漂移较低时，电解槽的共置进一步通过运营灵活性增加套利价值。

Conclusion: 所提框架能有效提升利润，且具有可解释性和风险感知能力，尤其适合分布漂移低的场景，混合电站中电解槽的灵活性可增强套利效果。

Abstract: Electricity markets increasingly expose stochastic energy generators to arbitrage opportunities between the day-ahead and balancing markets, driven by widening price spreads. However, opportunistic bidding, deliberately deviating from the production forecast to exploit anticipated price spreads, carries significant risk, and existing frameworks rarely offer explainable, risk-aware decision support. We propose a predict-then-contextual-optimize framework that decomposes the day-ahead bidding decision into three explicit stages to decide, when to engage in arbitrage, in what direction, and to what extent. A probabilistic binary classifier with confidence thresholds determines whether the predicted price spread is sufficiently confident to justify an opportunistic bid. Otherwise, the trader defaults to an arbitrage-free bid equal to the power forecast. A linear decision policy learned for each class via contextual optimization determines the magnitude of the bid deviation from the power forecast. The framework accommodates both standalone renewable generation and hybrid power plants combining renewable generation with other assets, such as an electrolyzer. We evaluate the framework on a real wind farm in the European bidding zones DK1 and DE/LU using a rolling-window procedure and compare it against several benchmark bidding strategies. The results show that the proposed framework increases mean profit relative to an arbitrage-free benchmark, reaching an improvement of about 7% for the hybrid power plant in DK1. The largest gains occur when distributional drift between training and testing windows is low, while the co-located electrolyzer further increases arbitrage value by providing additional operational flexibility.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学公式化的广义Prandtl-Ishlinskii停止算子虽有效捕捉迟滞非线性，但需要局部迭代更新每个迟滞子，计算开销大，因此需要简化以降低计算成本。

Method: 将停止算子上的非线性映射替换为恒等映射，直接对输出进行加权，同时保留由斜坡死区基函数表示的非线性无滞回响应。在各向同性情况下，得到局部塑性修正的闭式解，消除了逐迟滞子的牛顿迭代更新。

Result: 将简化后的本构映射集成到有限元求解器中，数值结果表明计算时间显著减少，且精度与广义模型相当。

Abstract: While the thermodynamically formulated generalized Prandtl-Ishlinskii stop-type operator effectively captures hysteresis nonlinearities, it requires a local iterative procedure to update each hysteron, resulting in considerable computational effort. In this work, we propose a simplified thermodynamic formulation of the generalized Prandtl-Ishlinskii stop operator. The nonlinear mapping on the stop operator is replaced by an identity, such that the hysteresis operators are directly weighted through their outputs, while the nonlinear anhysteretic response, represented by ramp dead-zone basis functions, is fully preserved. For isotropic cases, this simplification enables a closed-form solution for the local plastic correction, eliminating per-hysteron iterative Newton updates. The resulting constitutive mapping is integrated into a finite element solver, and numerical results show a significant reduction in computation time with accuracy comparable to the generalized model.
