### [145] [Near-Optimal Lower Bounds on One-Bit Compressed Sensing of Approximately Sparse Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06750)
*Junren Chen,Arya Mazumdar,Ming Yuan*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文为单比特压缩感知中近似稀疏信号的均匀欧几里得误差提供了首个近最优下界，证明了在子高斯测量矩阵下，下界至少为(k/m)^{1/3}（对数因子内），并通过扩展到ℓ_q球（q∈[0,1]）得到了连续的下界谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究中单比特压缩感知的最优上界为(k/m)^{1/3}，但缺乏匹配的下界，无法确认该上界是否紧；同时需要覆盖更广泛的近似稀疏信号假设（从精确k稀疏到ℓ_1球松弛），并统一两种主流模型（规范单比特模型与均匀抖动模型）。

Method: 首先将小欧几里得球嵌入信号集（均匀抖动模型直接嵌入，规范模型通过提升映射实现），然后在球内构造两个信号，它们欧几里得距离至少为(k/m)^{1/3}（对数因子内），但二进制测量结果无法区分；该论证进一步扩展到ℓ_q球（q∈[0,1]），得到下界Ω̃((k/m)^{(2-q)/(2+q)})，平滑连接q=0（精确稀疏）和q=1（ℓ_1稀疏）的情况。

Result: 建立了单比特压缩感知均匀欧几里得误差的近最优下界(k/m)^{1/3}，与已有上界相匹配；对于ℓ_q稀疏信号，下界为Ω̃((k/m)^{(2-q)/(2+q)})；结果还推广到sub-Weibull矩阵、对抗性比特翻转、矩阵恢复等场景，并刻画了非稀疏情形的转变。

Conclusion: 本文的下界表明已有上界（除对数因子外）是紧的，为单比特压缩感知的误差界提供了完整刻画；推广结果展示了该下界框架的普适性，可应用于多种扩展场景。

Abstract: This paper provides the first near-optimal lower bounds for one-bit compressed sensing of approximately sparse signals lying in a scaled $\ell_1$ ball, which is a commonly adopted relaxation of the exactly $k$-sparse assumption. In prior works, the best known upper bounds on uniform Euclidean error are of order $\widetilde{O}((k/m)^{1/3})$, where $m$ is the number of measurements. Under sub-Gaussian matrices, we establish nearly matching lower bounds for both the canonical one-bit compressed sensing model and the uniformly dithered model. Our argument is to first embed a small Euclidean ball into the signal set, which is straightforward for the dithered model but relies on a lifting map for the canonical model, and then construct two signals in this small ball that are separated in Euclidean distance by at least $(k/m)^{1/3}$ (up to logarithmic factor) but are indistinguishable from the binary measurements. Moreover, our argument extends to approximately sparse signals that live in a properly scaled $\ell_q$ ball $(q\in [0,1])$, yielding a lower bound $\widetildeΩ((k/m)^{\frac{2-q}{2+q}})$ that smoothly bridges the cases of exact sparsity ($q=0$) and $\ell_1$ sparsity ($q=1$). Finally, we discuss the extensions of our lower bounds to sub-Weibull matrices, adversarial bit flipping, matrix recovery, and characterize the transition to the non-sparse case.

The resulting joint optimization of device selection, receive beamforming, and pinching-antenna placement is highly nonconvex due to the intricate coupling among these system variables. To address this challenge, we develop AirPASS, an alternating optimization framework with two main components: a homotopy-Riemannian margin-consolidation method for device selection and receive beamforming under fixed PASS configuration, and a homotopy-assisted geometry optimization method for updating the pinching-antenna positions under fixed selected devices and beamformer. Experiments show that AirPASS consistently outperforms conventional co-located MIMO baselines, remains close to ideal FedAvg, and achieves an attractive performance-complexity tradeoff relative to SDR-DC and matching-pursuit scheduling alternatives.

### [148] [What Semivalues Cannot See: The Information Content of Anonymous Marginal Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07013)
*Matthew Fried*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文系统刻画了半值族的公共核：Harsanyi红利坐标下，所有半值的联合信息等价于每个玩家在每个联盟规模上的总协同效应，核即为闭环协同结构。主要结果包括：混合差分审计与红利切片谐波的精确对应；非零盲博弈违反超可加性、单调性和核心存在性；四类玩家起存在所有半值下价值相同但不同的凸博弈；正加权Shapley族达到完全信息$2^n-1$；规模$c$的联盟击败所有$\le d$阶审计当且仅当$c\ge2d+2$；$n=5$时存在非构造成票规则在所有半值权力指数下价值相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典合作博弈理论中，半值族（包括Shapley值、Banzhaf值等）共享一个非平凡公共核。Kleinberg和Weiss (1985)及Amer等人(2003)已证明该核从四玩家起非零，但Crisman和Orrison (2015)提出其内在结构问题悬而未决。本文旨在给出该核的具体结构刻画，并系统阐明半值族信息容量的边界与盲博弈的性质。

Method: 采用Harsanyi红利坐标将博弈分解为各阶协同效应；利用混合差分算子（order-$\le d$ mixed-difference audits）与红利切片谐波的对应关系建立形式化框架；通过构造性反例与维度计数证明各类存在性结果；结合线性代数与组合方法计算各阶审计的精确维度；枚举$n=5$所有简单博弈进行实证普查。

Result: （1）混合差分审计精确恢复度$\le d$的红利切片谐波，各阶维度有闭式解；（2）非零盲博弈违反超可加性、单调性及核心存在性；（3）四玩家起存在半值等值但不同的凸博弈，具精确摄动阈值；（4）正加权Shapley族信息完整（$2^n-1$），匿名性为边际框架内的约束公理；（5）联盟规模$c\ge2d+2$时击败所有$\le d$阶审计；（6）$n=5$时存在非构造成票规则在所有半值权力指数下碰撞，但无加权博弈参与碰撞；（7）经典合作博弈对半值族可见度$0.90-1.00$，随机博弈仅$0.089$。

Conclusion: 半值族公共核的协同闭环结构已完全阐明；匿名性是半值族信息完整的唯一约束公理；加权博弈在碰撞中具有刚性；经典博弈因结构化设计而具有高可见度，随机博弈几乎完全不可见。该研究为合作博弈的审计、权力指数比较与博弈分类提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The semivalue family shares a common kernel: games invisible to every anonymous marginal value at once, nonzero from four players (Kleinberg and Weiss, 1985; Amer, Derks and Giménez, 2003). Crisman and Orrison (2015) ask what useful structure this kernel carries; this paper gives a concrete answer. In Harsanyi-dividend coordinates the joint information of all semivalues is exactly each player's total synergy at each coalition size, so the kernel is synergy arranged in closed circuits. We prove: order-$\le d$ mixed-difference audits recover exactly the degree-$\le d$ dividend-slice harmonics, with closed-form dimension at every rung; nonzero blind games fail superadditivity, monotonicity, and core existence, yet distinct convex games with identical values under every semivalue exist from four players, with exact perturbation thresholds; the positive weighted Shapley family attains full information $2^n-1$, so anonymity is the binding axiom within the marginal framework; and a coalition of size $c$ defeats every audit of order $\le d$ precisely when $c\ge2d+2$, within the convex class for small perturbations. An exhaustive census at $n=5$ exhibits non-isomorphic voting rules with identical values under every semivalue power index; no weighted game participates in any collision, prompting a swing-rigidity conjecture. Measured against the theory, classical cooperative games sit at $0.90$ to $1.00$ visibility to the family versus $0.089$ for a random game.

</details>


### [149] [Simple Nash Equilibria for Qualitative Multiplayer Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07151)
*Mona Alluwaym,James C. A. Main,Sven Schewe*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了回合制确定性游戏中ω-正则目标下纳什均衡和子博弈完美均衡的记忆需求，证明了在可达性、安全性及0-2 Muller目标（接受集向上或向下封闭）及其组合中，始终存在无记忆随机化（即平稳）子博弈完美均衡，并给出了构造算法。同时揭示了随机化在部分目标中的必要性，以及无记忆均衡在其他Muller目标类中的不存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论分析与算法构造相结合的方法，针对可达性、安全性、0-2 Muller目标（向上/向下封闭）等目标类，证明无记忆随机化子博弈完美均衡的存在性并设计构造算法；同时通过反例论证随机化的必要性及无记忆均衡的不存在性。

Result: 1) 在可达性、安全性及0-2 Muller目标（接受集向上或向下封闭）及其任意组合中，始终存在无记忆随机化子博弈完美均衡；2) 随机化在可达性/ Büchi及安全性/ CoBüchi目标中是构造无记忆均衡的必要条件；3) 相对于Mostowski层级，其他Muller目标类中无记忆均衡不存在。

Conclusion: 无记忆随机化均衡的存在性界限与Muller目标的层级结构紧密相关，仅在特定目标类中成立，且随机化在某些情况下不可或缺。

Abstract: We investigate memory requirements for Nash and subgame-perfect equilibria in turn-based deterministic games with $ω$-regular objectives. We prove that memoryless randomised (i.e., stationary) subgame-perfect equilibria always exist in games with reachability, safety, and 0-2 Muller objectives (i.e., Muller objectives for which accepting sets are either up- or downward closed), and any combination of these objectives. We provide an algorithm to construct such an equilibrium. We also show that randomisation may be required to construct memoryless equilibria in games with reachability or Büchi as well as safety or CoBüchi objectives, and that memoryless equilibria need not exist for any other class of Muller objectives (with respect to the Mostowski hierarchy).

Method: 利用稳定匹配集的旋转偏序集表示，特别是每个代理人受影响的旋转在该偏序集中形成链这一性质，设计了多项式时间算法；同时通过与最小割可表示性框架的对比及子模函数最小化解释来定位方法的理论边界。

Result: 对两种平衡度量（最大-最小差值、比率）均给出了多项式时间算法；证明了该目标不被现有最小割可表示性框架所覆盖，并识别出了一个可归约为子模函数最小化的特例。

Conclusion: 本文在理论上拓展了稳定匹配问题的优化目标，为在保证稳定性的前提下实现代理人效用均衡提供了高效求解方法，其旋转链性质是算法设计的关键结构性洞察。

Abstract: We introduce the Stable Matching Problem with Minimum Utility Gap, which seeks a stable matching in which the utilities received by individual agents are as balanced as possible. Our framework can handle many-to-many matchings and general utility functions on partner sets that are consistent with the agents' preferences. We consider two measures for comparing agents' utilities: the difference between the maximum and minimum utilities, and their ratio.
  We provide a polynomial-time algorithm for both versions. The algorithm exploits the rotation-poset representation of the set of stable matchings and, in particular, the fact that the rotations affecting each agent form a chain in this poset. To position our result, we also clarify its relation to existing frameworks: we show that our objectives are not captured by the recent minimum-cut representability framework, while identifying a special case that admits a submodular function minimization interpretation.

</details>


### [151] [Positional Determinacy with Colored Vertices: a 1-to-2-Player Lift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07415)
*Raphaël Berthon,Stéphane Le Roux*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文证明了在顶点染色游戏中，对于任何前缀独立的目标W，以下三者等价：(1) W在所有顶点染色单人游戏中是位置确定的；(2) W在所有顶点染色双人游戏中是位置确定的；(3) W等价于关于有序颜色对的奇偶性目标。同时证明了颜色集合的有限性是该等价关系成立的必要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解哪类颜色目标能保证位置确定性是博弈论中的基础问题。已有工作证明了边染色游戏中与奇偶性目标的等价关系，本文希望将这一结论推广到顶点染色游戏，并建立两种染色框架之间的对应关系。

Method: 通过证明三者之间的蕴含关系来建立等价性，具体包括：(1)从单人位置确定性推导出双人位置确定性（1-to-2-player lift）；(2)从双人位置确定性推导出目标等价于有序颜色对上的奇偶性目标；(3)反向蕴含关系。同时通过构造反例证明颜色集合有限性是必要条件。

Result: 成功证明了顶点染色游戏中三类位置确定性条件与奇偶性目标的等价关系，并证明了该等价关系依赖颜色集合的有限性。此外，建立了边染色游戏与顶点染色游戏之间的双向对应关系。

Conclusion: 顶点染色游戏中的前缀独立位置确定性目标本质上等价于有序颜色对上的奇偶性目标，且颜色集合有限性不可放松。所发展的技术方法为两种染色框架之间的转换提供了新途径。

Abstract: Positional determinacy of vertex-colored parity games was proved in the 1990s, which directly implies positional determinacy of edge-colored parity games. In 2006, it was shown that if a prefix-independent color-based objective ensures that every edge-colored two-player turn-based game is positionally determined, this objective is equivalent to a parity objective. We prove a similar result for vertex-colored games, namely that the following are equivalent for any prefix-independent objective $W$ over a finite set of colors:
  - $W$ is positionally determined on all vertex-colored one-player games.
  - $W$ is positionally determined on all vertex-colored two-player games.
  - $W$ is equivalent to a parity objective on ordrerd pairs of colors.
  We prove that finiteness of the color set is required for our equivalence to hold. Beyond this $1$-to-$2$-player lift, the technique that we develop to handle the pairs of colors establishes a promising 2-way correspondence between edge-colored games and vertex-colored games.

</details>


### [152] [FedMark-FM: Auditable, Risk-Adjusted Data Markets for Federated Foundation-Model Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07529)
*Phat T. Tran-Truong,Xuan-Bach Le,Minh Nhat Nguyen*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出FedMark-FM，一个面向联邦基础模型适配的可审计、风险调整的数据市场框架，通过分层不确定性感知的Shapley估值(S3Val)、管道顺序估值和预算可行支付机制，解决异构贡献、隐私约束和策略性行为问题。实验表明在下游准确率、战略客户端筛选和校准覆盖率上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习激励机制将客户端视为同质的数据或更新提供者，这与基础模型适配管道中贡献异构、非IID、管道依赖、隐私受限且易受策略性行为影响的现实严重不匹配。

Method: 提出FedMark-FM框架：1) 将客户端建模为类型化人工制品的卖方；2) 设计S3Val（分层不确定性感知Shapley估值器），支持管道顺序估值；3) 将下置信界值转化为预算可行支付，惩罚重复、Sybil分裂、投毒适配器、隐私预算博弈和成本膨胀。

Result: 在提示注入投毒者场景下，FedMark-FM较volume、留一法和FL-Shapley提升下游准确率7.5-8.1个百分点，且零个策略性客户端被选中。分裂保形校准在均值宽度0.0141处达到完整下界覆盖（朴素区间为0.33）。管道顺序估值与无序估值的Spearman相关系数为0.76，选中集合重叠度为0.67。

Conclusion: 联邦基础模型的激励机制可以设计为可审计的数据基础设施，耦合估值、机制设计、隐私接口和管道顺序语义。FedMark-FM证明了这一方向的可行性。

Abstract: Federated foundation-model adaptation increasingly relies on heterogeneous private artifacts (retrieval corpora, prompts and demonstrations, LoRA adapters, preference and safety data, and update sketches), yet existing federated-learning incentive mechanisms price clients as homogeneous data or update providers. This assumption poorly matches foundation-model pipelines, where contribution value is heterogeneous, non-IID, pipeline-dependent, privacy-constrained, and vulnerable to strategic behavior. We propose FedMark-FM, an auditable, risk-adjusted data-market framework that models clients as sellers of typed artifacts, estimates marginal contribution with S3Val, a stratified, uncertainty-aware Shapley estimator supporting pipeline-ordered valuation, and converts lower-confidence-bound values into budget-feasible payments penalizing duplication, sybil splitting, poisoned adapters, privacy-budget gaming, and cost inflation. We evaluate FedMark-FM-Bench across FEVER retrieval, held-out generator-backed RAG, and trained PEFT/LoRA tracks. Under a held-out prompt-injection poisoner, FedMark-FM improves downstream accuracy by 7.5-8.1 points over volume, leave-one-out, and FL-Shapley while selecting zero strategic clients. Split-conformal calibration reaches full lower-bound coverage at mean width 0.0141, versus 0.33 for naive intervals. We prove pipeline-ordered valuation is the unique credit rule respecting serving causality, and show it materially changes credit assignment (Spearman 0.76, selected-set overlap 0.67) while leaving held-out task quality unchanged; the market preserves rare specialists with audit-ready ledgers at 200-1000-client scale. FedMark-FM shows incentives for federated foundation models can be engineered as auditable data infrastructure coupling valuation, mechanism design, privacy interfaces, and pipeline-order semantics.

</details>
